Bhk māmupāsta didṛkṣāvān yāṣṭīkavyāhato hariḥ
Bhk ājñālābhonmukho dūrāt kākṣeṇā 'nādarekṣitaḥ
Bhk virugṇodagraghārā'gnaḥ kuliśo mama vakṣasi
Bhk abhinnaṃ śatadhā ''tmānaṃ manyate balinaṃ balī
Bhk kṛtvā laṅkādrumā''lānamahamairāvataṃ gajam
Bhk bandhane 'nupayogitvān nataṃ tṛṇavadatyajam
Bhk āhopuruṣikāṃ paśya mama
sadratnakāntibhiḥ
Bhk dhvastā'ndhakāre 'pi pure pūrṇendoḥ sannidhiḥ sadā
Bhk hṛtaratnaś cyutodyogo rakṣobhyaḥ karado divi
Bhk pūtakratāyīmabhyeti satrapaḥ kiṃ na gotrabhit
Bhk atulyamahasā sārdhaṃ rāmeṇa mama vigrahaḥ
Bhk trapākaras
tathāpyeṣa yatiṣye tadvinigrahe
Bhk utpatya khaṃ daśagrīvo manoyāyī śitā'strabhṛt
Bhk samudrasavidhā''vāsaṃ mārīcaṃ prati cakrame

Bhk antardhatsva raghuvyāghrāt tasmāt tvaṃ rākṣaseśvara 
Bhk yo raṇne durupasthāno hastarodhaṃ dadhad dhanuḥ

Bhk yamā''syadṛśvarī tasya tāḍakā vetti vikramam
Bhk śūraṃmanyo raṇāc cā'haṃ nirastaḥ siṃhanardinā

nā 'nvabhāvi tvayā 'pyasau

yānagopīn makheṣu saḥ

mā ''rabdhā balivigraham

Bhk yātayāmaṃ vijitavān sa rāmaṃ yadi kiṃ tataḥ
Bhk aghāni tāḍakā tena lajjābhayavibhūṣaṇā
Bhk strījane yadi tac chlāghyaṃ
dhig lokaṃ kṣudramānasam
Bhk yad gehenardinamasau śarair bhīrumabhāyayat
Bhk kubrahmayajñake rāmo bhavantaṃ
pauruṣaṃ na tat
Bhk cirakāloṣitaṃ jīrṇaṃ kīṭaniṣkuṣitaṃ dhanuḥ
Bhk kiṃ citraṃ yadi rāmeṇa bhagnaṃ kṣatriyakā'ntike
Bhk vanatāpasake vīrau vipakṣe galitā''darau
Bhk kiṃ citraṃ yadi sā'vajñau mamratuḥ kharadūṣaṇau

nityaṃ śaraṇakāmyasi

stauṣi śatrūṃś ca naḥ sadā

Bhk kārayiṣyāmi vā kṛtyaṃ vijighṛkṣur vanaukasau

jalaśuciḥ śuddhadan rāvaṇaḥ śikhī

niranvayajane vane

Bhk sukṛtaṃ priyakārī tvaṃ kaṃ harasyupatiṣṭhase

chinadmi kṣaṇadācarān
Bhk yamaṃ yunajmi kālena samindhāno 'strakauśalam
Bhk śuṣkapeṣaṃ pinaṣmyurvīmakhindānaḥ svatejasā
Bhk bhūtiṃ tṛṇadmi yakṣāṇāṃ
hinasmīndrasya vikramam
Bhk bhanajmi sarvamaryādās
tanacmi vyoma vistṛtam
Bhk na tṛṇehmīti loko 'yaṃ māṃ vinte niṣparākram
Bhk evaṃ vadan dāśarathirapṛṇag dhanuśā śaraṃ
Bhk nyavartayat sumitrābhūs taṃ cikīrṣuṃ jagatkṣayam
Bhk aikṣetāmāśramādārād girikalpaṃ patatriṇam
Bhk taṃ sītāghātinaṃ matvā hantuṃ rāmo 'bhyadhāvata
Bhk mā vadhiṣṭhā jaṭāyuṃ māṃ sītāṃ rāmā 'hamaikṣiṣi
Bhk upāsthitaivamukte taṃ sakhāyaṃ rāghavaḥ pituḥ
Bhk papraccha jānakīvārtāṃ saṃgrāmaṃ ca patatriṇam
tato rāvaṇamākhyāya dviṣantaṃ patatāṃ varaḥ
Bhk vraṇavedanayā glāyan mamāra girikandare
Bhk tasyāgnyambukriyāṃ kṛtvā pratasthāte punar vanam
Bhk satvānajasraṃ ghoreṇa balā'pakarṣamaśnatā
Bhk kṣudhyatā jagṛhāte tau rakṣasā dīrghabāhunā
Bhk bhujau cakṛtatus tasya nistriṃśābhyāṃ raghūttmau
Bhk sa chinnabāhurapatad vihvalo hvalayan bhuvam
iti prakīrṇakāḥ
atha kṛtyā'dhikāraḥ
Bhk praṣṭavyaṃ pṛcchatas tasya kathanīyamavīvacat
Bhk ātmānaṃ vanavāsaṃ ca jeyaṃ cā 'riṃ raghūttamaḥ
Bhk labhyā kathaṃ nu vaidehī
śakyo draṣṭuṃ kathaṃ ripuḥ
Bhk sahyaḥ kathaṃ viyogaś ca
gadyametat tvayā mama
Bhk ahaṃ rāma 
śriyaḥ putro madyapīta iva bhraman
Bhk pāpacaryo muneḥ śāpāj jāta ityavadat sa tam
Bhk prayātas tava yamyatvaṃ śastrapūto bravīmi te
Bhk rāvaṇena hṛtā sītā laṅkāṃ nītā surāriṇā
Bhk ṛṣyamūke 'navadyo 'sti paṇyabhrātṛvadhaḥ kapiḥ
Bhk sugrīvo nāma
varyo 'sau bhavatā cāruvikramaḥ
Bhk tena vahyena hantāsi tvamaryaṃ puruṣā'śinām
Bhk rākṣasaṃ krūrakarmāṇaṃ śakrā'riṃ dūravāsinam
Bhk āste smaran sa kāntāyā hṛtāyā vālinā kapiḥ
Bhk vṛṣo yathopasaryāyā goṣṭhe gor daṇḍatāḍitaḥ
Bhk tena saṅgatamāryeṇa rāmā 'jaryaṃ kuru drutam
Bhk laṅkāṃ prāpya tataḥ pāpaṃ daśagrīvaṃ haniṣyasi
Bhk anṛtodyaṃ na tatrāsti
satyavadyaṃ bravīmyaham
Bhk mitrabhūyaṃ gatas tasya ripuhatyāṃ kariṣyasi
Bhk ādṛtyas tena vṛtyena stutyo juṣyeṇa saṃgataḥ
Bhk ityaḥ śiṣyeṇa guruvad gṛdhyamarthamavāpsyasi
Bhk nā'kheyaḥ sāgaro 'pyanyas tasya sadbhṛtyaśālinaḥ
Bhk manyus tasya tvayā mārgyo
mṛjyaḥ śokaś ca tena te
Bhk sa rājasūyayājīva tejasā sūryasannibhaḥ
Bhk amṛṣodyaṃ vadan rucyo jagāhe dyāṃ niśācaraḥ
Bhk akṛṣṭapacyāḥ paśyantau tato dāśarathī latāḥ
Bhk ratnā'nnapānakupyānāmāṭatur naṣṭasaṃsmṛtī
Bhk samuttarantāvavyathyau nadān bhidyoddhyasannibhān
Bhk sidhyatārāmiva khyātāṃ śabarīmāpatur vane
Bhk vasānāṃ valkale śūddhe vipūyaiḥ kṛtamekhalām
Bhk kṣāmāmañjanapiṇḍā''bhā daṇdinīmajinā ''starām
Bhk pragṛhyapadavat sādhvīṃ spaṣṭarūpāmavikriyām
Bhk agṛhyāṃ vītakāmatvād devagṛhyāmaninditām
Bhk dharmakṛtyaratāṃ nityamakṛṣyaphalabhojanām
Bhk dṛṣṭvā tāmamucad rāmo yugyā''yāta iva śramam
Bhk sa tāmūce 'thakaccit tvamamāvāsyāsamanvaye
Bhk pit ṇāṃ kuruṣe kāryamapākyaiḥ svādubhiḥ phalaiḥ
Bhk avaśyapāvyaṃ pavase kaccit tvaṃ devabhāgghviḥ
Bhk āsāvyamadhvare somaṃ dvijaiḥ kaccin namasyasi
Bhk ācāmyaṃ saṃdhyayoḥ kaccit satyak te na prahīyate
Bhk kaccidagnimivā ''nāyyaṃ kāle saṃmanyase 'tithim
Bhk na praṇāyyo janaḥ kaccin nikāyyaṃ te 'dhitiṣṭhati
Bhk devakāryavighātāya dharmadrohī mahodaye 
Bhk kuṇḍapāyyavatāṃ kaccidagnicityāvatāṃ tathā
Bhk kathābhī ramase nityamupacāyyavatāṃ śubhe 
atha prakīrṇakāḥ
Bhk vardhate te tapo bhīru 
vyajeṣṭhā vighnanāyakān
Bhk ajaiṣīḥ kāmasaṃmohau
saṃprāpthā vinayena vā
Bhk nā ''yasyasi tapasyantī
gurūn samyagatūtuṣaḥ
Bhk yamān nodavijiṣṭhās tvaṃ
nijāya tapase 'tuṣaḥ
Bhk athā'rdhyaṃ madhuparkā''dyamupanīyā ''darādasau
Bhk arcayitvā phalairarcyau sarvatrā ''khyadanāmayam
ataḥ paraṃ kṛdadhikāraḥ
Bhk sakhyasya tava sugrīvaḥ kārakaḥ kapinandanaḥ
Bhk drutaṃ draṣṭāsi maithilpāḥ
 saivamuktvā tiro 'bhavat
Bhk nandanāni munīndrāṇāṃ ramaṇāni vanaukasām
Bhk vanāni bhejatur vīrau tataḥ pāmpāni rāghavau
Bhk bhṛṅgā''līkokilakruṅbhir vāśanaiḥ paśya lakṣmaṇa 
Bhk rocanair bhūṣitāṃ pampā masmākaṃ hṛdayāvidham
Bhk paribhāvīṇi tārāṇāṃ paśya manthīni cetasām
Bhk udbhāsīni jalejāni dunvantyadayitaṃ janam
Bhk sarvatra dayitā'dhīnaṃ suvyaktaṃ rāmaṇīyakam
Bhk yena jātaṃ priyā'pāye kadvadaṃ haṃsakokilam
Bhk pakṣibhir vitṛdair yūnā śākhibhiḥ kusumotkiraiḥ
Bhk ajño yo yasya vā nā 'sti priyaḥ
praglo bhaven na saḥ
Bhk dhvanīnāmuddhamairebhir madhūnāmuddhayair bhṛśam
Bhk ājighraiḥ puṣpagandhānāṃ patagair glapitā vayam
Bhk dhārayaiḥ kusumormīṇāṃ pārayair bādhituṃ janān
Bhk śākhibhir hā hatā bhūyo hṛdayānāmudejayaiḥ
Bhk dadair duḥkhasya mādṛgbhyo dhāyairāmodamuttamam
Bhk limpairiva tanor vātaiś cetayaḥ syāj jvalo na kaḥ
Bhk avaśyāyakaṇā''srāvāś cārumuktāphalatviṣaḥ
Bhk kurvanti cittasaṃsrāvaṃ calatparṇā'grasaṃbhṛtāḥ
Bhk avasāyo bhaviṣyāmi duḥkhasyā 'sya kadā nvaham
Bhk na jīvasyā 'vahāro māṃ karoti sukhinaṃ yamaḥ
Bhk dahye 'haṃ madhuno lehair dāvairugrair yathā giriḥ
Bhk nāyaḥ ko'tra sa
yena syāṃ batā 'haṃ vigatajvaraḥ
Bhk samāviṣṭaṃ graheṇeva grāheṇevā ''ttamarṇave
Bhk dṛṣṭvā gṛhān smarasyeva vanā'ntān mama mānasam
Bhk vātā''haticalacchākhā nartakā iva śākhinaḥ
Bhk duḥsahā hī parikṣiptāḥ kvaṇadbhiraligāthakaiḥ
Bhk ekahāyanasāraṅgagatī raghukulottamau
Bhk lavakau śatruśaktīnāmṛṣyamūkamagacchatām
Bhk tau vālipraṇidhī matvā sugrīvo 'cintayat kapiḥ
Bhk bandhunā vigṛhīto'haṃ bhūyāsaṃ jīvakaḥ katham
Bhk sa śatrulāvau manvāno rāghavau malayaṃ girim
Bhk jagāma saparīvāro vyomamāyamivotthitam
Bhk śarmadaṃ mārutiṃ dūtaṃ viṣamasthaḥ kapidvipam
Bhk śokā'panudamavyagraṃ prāyuṅkta kapikuñjaraḥ
Bhk viśvāsapradaveṣo 'sau pathiprajñaḥ samāhitaḥ
Bhk cittasaṃkhyo jigīṣūṇāmutpapāta nabhastalam
Bhk surāpairiva ghūrṇadbhiḥ śākhibhiḥ pavanā''hataiḥ
Bhk ṛṣyamūkamagād bhṛṅgaiḥ pragītaṃ sāmagairiva
Bhk taṃ manoharamāgatya giriṃ varmaharau kapiḥ
Bhk vīrau sukhā ''haro 'vocad bhikṣur bhikṣārhavigrahaḥ
Bhk balināvamūmadrīndraṃ yuvāṃ stamberamāviva
Bhk ācakṣāthāṃ mithaḥ kasmācchaṅkareṇā 'pi durgamam
Bhk vyāptaṃ guhāśayaiḥ krūraiḥ kravyādbhiḥ saniśācaraiḥ
Bhk tuṅgaśailataruchannaṃ mānuṣāṇāmagocaram
Bhk satvamejayasiṃhā''ḍhyān stanaṃdhāyasamatviṣau
Bhk kathaṃ nāḍiṃdhamān mārgānāgatau viṣamopalān
Bhk attīrṇau vā kathaṃ bhīmāḥ saritaḥ kūlamudvahāḥ
Bhk āsāditau kathaṃ brūtaṃ na gajaiḥ kūlamudrujaiḥ
Bhk rāmo 'vocaddhanūmantam āvāmabhraṃlihaṃ girim
Bhk aiva vidvan
pituḥ kāmāt pāntāvalpaṃpacān munīn
Bhk amitaṃpacamīśānaṃ sarvabhogīṇamuttamam
Bhk āvayoḥ pitaraṃ viddhi khyātaṃ daśarthaṃ bhuvi
Bhk chalena dayitā 'raṇyād rakṣasā 'ruṃtudena naḥ
Bhk asūryaṃpaśyayā mūrtyā hṛtā
tāṃ mṛgayāvahe
Bhk pratyūce māruti rāmam  asti vālīti vānaraḥ
Bhk śamayedapi saṃgrāme yo lalāṭaṃtapaṃ ravim
Bhk ugraṃpaśyena sugrīvas tena bhrātā nirākṛtaḥ
Bhk tasya mitrīyato dūtaḥ saṃprāpto 'smi vaśaṃvadaḥ
Bhk priyaṃvado 'pi naivā 'haṃ bruve mithyā paraṃtapa 
Bhk sakhyā tena daśagrīvaṃ nihantāsi dviṣaṃtapam
Bhk vācaṃyamo'hamanṛte satyametad bravīmi te
Bhk ehi sarvaṃsahaṃ mitraṃ sugrīvaṃ kuru vānaram
Bhk sarvaṃkaṣayaśaḥśākhaṃ rāmakalpataruṃ kapiḥ
Bhk ādāyā' bhraṃkaṣaṃ prāyān malayaṃ phalaśālinam
Bhk meghaṃkaramivāyāntamṛtuṃ rāmaṃ klamānvitāḥ
Bhk dṛṣṭvā mene nasugrīvo vālibhānuṃ bhayaṃkaram
Bhk upāgnyakurutāṃ sakhyamanyonyasya priyaṃkarau
Bhk kṣemaṃkarāṇi kāryāṇi paryālocayatāṃ tataḥ
Bhk āśitaṃbhavamutkruṣṭaṃ valgitaṃ śayitaṃ sthitam
Bhk bahvamanyata kākutsthaḥ kapīnāṃ svecchayā kṛtam
Bhk tato baliṃdamaprakhyaṃ kapiviśvaṃbharā'dhipam
Bhk sugrīvaḥ prābravīd rāmaṃ vālino yudhi vikramam
Bhk vasuṃdharāyāṃ kṛtsnāyāṃ nā'sti vālisamo balī
Bhk hṛdayaṃgamametat tvāṃ bravīmi
na parābhavam
Bhk dūragairantagair bāṇair bhavānatyantagaḥ śriyaḥ
Bhk api saṃkrandanasya syāt kruddhaḥ
kimuta vālinaḥ
Bhk vareṇa tu muner vālī saṃjāto dasyuho raṇe
Bhk avāryaprasaraḥ prātarudyanniva tamo'pahaḥ
Bhk atipriyatvān na hi me kātaraṃ pratipadyate
Bhk ceto vālivadhaṃ rāma 
kleśāpahamupasthitam
Bhk śīrṣaghātinamāyātamarīṇāṃ tvāṃ vilokayan
Bhk patighnīlakṣmaṇopatāṃ manye'haṃ vālinaḥ śriyam
Bhk śatrughnān yudhi hastighno girīn kṣipyannakṛtrimān
Bhk śilpibhiḥ pāṇighaiḥ kruddhas tvayā jayyo 'bhyupāyavān
Bhk āḍhyaṃkaraṇavikrānto mahiṣasya suradviṣaḥ
Bhk priyaṃkaraṇamindrasya duṣkaraṃ kṛtavān vadham
Bhk priyaṃbhāvukatāṃ yātas taṃ kṣipan yojanaṃ mṛtam
Bhk svarge priyaṃbhaviṣṇuś ca krtsnaṃ śakto 'pyabādhayan
Bhk jijñāsoḥ śaktimastrāṇāṃ rāmo nyūnadhiyaḥ kapeḥ
Bhk abhīnat pratipattyarthaṃ sapta vyoma spṛśas tarūn
Bhk tato vālipaśau vadhye rāmartvigjitasādhvasaḥ
Bhk abhyabhūn nilayaṃ bhrātuḥ sugrīvo ninadan dadhṛk
Bhk guhāyā niragād vālī siṃho mṛgamiva dyuvan
Bhk bhrātaraṃ yuṅ bhiyaḥ saṃkhye ghoṣeṇā ''pūrayan diśaḥ
Bhk vyāyacchamānayor mūḍho bhede sadṛśayos tayoḥ
Bhk bāṇamudyatamāyaṃsīdikṣvākukulanandanaḥ
Bhk ṛṣyamūkamagāt klantaḥ kapir mṛgasadṛg drutam
Bhk kiṣkindhā'drisadā''tyarthaṃ niṣpiṣṭaḥ koṣṇamucchvasan
Bhk kṛtvā vālidruhaṃ rāmo mālayā saviśeṣaṇam
Bhk aṅgadasvaṃ punar hantuṃ kapighnā''hvāyayad raṇe
Bhk tayor vānarasenānyoḥ saṃprahāre tanucchidam
Bhk vālino dūrabhāg rāmo bāṇaṃ prāṇā'damatyajat
Bhk vālinaṃ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā vānarā ripughātinam
Bhk bāndhavā''krośino bhejuranāthāḥ kakubho daśa
Bhk dhig dāśarathimityūcur munayo vanavartinaḥ
Bhk upeyur madhupāyinyaḥ krośantyas taṃ kapistriyaḥ
Bhk rāmamuccairupālabdha śūramānī kapiprabhuḥ
Bhk vraṇavedanayā glāyansādhuṃmanyamasādhuvat
Bhk mṛṣā 'si tvaṃ haviryājī rāghava 
chadmatāpasaḥ
Bhk anyavyāsaktaghātitvād brahmaghnāṃ pāpasaṃmitaḥ
Bhk pāpakṛt sukṛtāṃ madhye rājñaḥ puṇyakṛtaḥ sutaḥ
Bhk māmapāpaṃ durācāra 
kiṃ nihatyā 'bhidhāsyasi
Bhk agnicit somasud rājā rathacakracidā''diṣu
Bhk analeṣviṣṭavān kasmān na tvayā 'pekṣitaḥ pitā
Bhk māṃsavikrayiṇaḥ karma vyādhasyā 'pi vigarhitam
Bhk māṃ ghnatā bhavatā 'kāri niḥṣaṅkaṃ pāpadṛṣvanā
Bhk buddhipūrvaṃ dhruvan na tvā rājakṛtvā pitā khalam
Bhk sahayudhvānamanyena yo 'hino māmanāgasam
Bhk pañca pañcanakhā bhakṣyā ye proktāḥ kṛtajair dvijaiḥ
Bhk kauśalyāja 
śaśā''dīnāṃ teṣāṃ naiko 'pyahaṃ kapiḥ
Bhk kathaṃ duṣṭhuḥ svayaṃ dharme prajās tvaṃ pālayiṣyasi
Bhk ātmā'nujasya jihreṣi saumitres tvaṃ kathaṃ na vā
Bhk manye kiṃjamahaṃ ghnantaṃ tvāmakṣattriyaje raṇe
Bhk lakṣmaṇā 'dhija 
durvṛtta 
prayuktamanujena naḥ
Bhk pratyūce vālinaṃ rāmonā 'kṛtaṃ kṛtavānaham
Bhk yajvabhiḥ sutvabhiḥ pūvair jaradbhiś ca kapīṣvara 
Bhk te hi jālair gale pāśais tiraścāmupaseduṣām
Bhk ūṣuṣāṃ paradāraiś ca sārdhaṃ nidhanamaiṣiṣuḥ
Bhk ahaṃ tu ṣuṣruvānbhrātrā striyaṃ bhuktāṃ kanīyasā
Bhk upeyivānanūcānair ninditastvaṃ latāmṛga 
Bhk anvanaiṣīt tato vālī trapāvāniva rāghavam
Bhk nyakṣipac cā'ṅgadaṃ yatnāt kākutsthe tanayaṃ priyaṃ
Bhk mriyamāṇaḥ sa sugrīvaṃ proce sadbhāvamāgataḥ
Bhk saṃbhāviṣyāva ekasyāmabhijānāsi mātari
Bhk avasāva nagendreṣu
yat pāsyāvo madhūni ca
Bhk abhijānīhi tat sarvaṃ
bandhūnāṃ samayo hyayam
Bhk daivaṃ na vidadhe nūnaṃ yugapat sukhamāvayoḥ
Bhk śaśvad bahūva tad duḥsthaṃ yato na itihā 'karot
Bhk dadau sa dayitāṃ bhrātre mālāṃ cā'gryāṃ hiraṇmayīm
Bhk rājyaṃ saṃdiśya bhogāmś ca mamāra vraṇapīḍitaḥ
Bhk tasya nirvartya kartavyaṃ sugrīvo rāghavā''jñayā
Bhk kiṣkindhā'driguhāṃ gantuṃ manaḥ praṇidadhe drutam
Bhk nāmagrāhaṃ kapibhiraśanaiḥ stūyamānaḥ samantā danvagbhāvaṃ raghuvṛṣabhayor vānarendro virājan
Bhk abhyarṇe 'mbhaḥpatanasamaye parṇalībhūtasānuṃ kiṣkindhādriṃ nyaviśata madhukṣībaguñjaddvirepham
Bhk
Bhk tataḥ kartā vanā''kampaṃ vavau varṣāprabhañjanaḥ
Bhk nabhaḥ pūrayitāraś ca samunnemuḥ payodharāḥ
Bhk tarpaṇaṃ prajaniṣṇūnāṃ ṣasyānāmamalaṃ payaḥ
Bhk rociṣṇavaḥ savisphūrjā mumucur bhinnavad ghanāḥ
Bhk nirākariṣṇavo bhānuṃ divaṃ vartiṣṇavo 'bhitaḥ
Bhk alaṃkariṣṇavo bhāntas taḍitvantaś cariṣṇavaḥ
Bhk tān vilokyā 'sahiṣṇuḥ san vilalānponmadiṣṇuvat
Bhk vasan mālyavati glāsnū rāmo jiṣṇuradhṛṣṇuvat
Bhk bhramī kadambasaṃbhinnaḥ pavanaḥ śamināmapi
Bhk klamitvaṃ kurute'tyarthaṃ meghaśīkaraśītalaḥ
Bhk saṃjvāriṇeva manasā dhvāntamāyāsinā mayā
Bhk drohi khadyotasaṃparki nayanā'moṣi duḥsaham
Bhk kurvanti parisāriṇyo vidyutaḥ paridevinam
Bhk abhyāghātibhirāmiśrāś cātakaiḥ parirāṭibhiḥ
Bhk saṃsargī paridāhīva śīto 'pyābhāti śīkaraḥ
Bhk soḍhumākrīḍino 'śakyāḥ śikhinaḥ parivādinaḥ
Bhk etā devānurodhinyo dveṣiṇya iva rāgiṇam
Bhk pīḍayanti janaṃ dhārāḥ patantyo 'napakāriṇam
Bhk kūryād yoginamapyeṣa sphūrjāvān parimohinam
Bhk tyāginaṃ sukhaduḥkhasya parikṣepyambhasāmṛtuḥ
Bhk vikatthī yācate prattamaviśrambhī muhur jalam
Bhk parjanyaṃ cātakaḥ pakṣī nikṛntanniva mānasam
Bhk pralāpino bhaviṣyanti kadā nvete 'palāṣiṇaḥ
Bhk pramāthino viyuktānāṃ hiṃsakāḥ pāpadardurāḥ
Bhk nindako rajaniṃmanyaṃ divasaṃ kleśako niśām
Bhk prāvṛṣyanaiṣīt kākutsthaḥ kathaṃcit paridevakaḥ
Bhk athopaśarade 'paśyat krauñcānāṃ ceṣṭanaiḥ kulaiḥ
Bhk utkaṇṭhāvardhanaiḥ śubhraṃ ravaṇairambaraṃ tatam
Bhk vilokya dyotanaṃ candraṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ śocano 'vadat
Bhk paśya dandramaṇān haṃsānaravindasamutsukān
Bhk kapiś caṅkramaṇo 'dyāpi nā 'sau bhavati gardhanaḥ
Bhk kurvanti kopanaṃ tārā maṇḍanā gaganasya mām
Bhk nā 'vaityāpyāyitāraṃ kiṃ kamalāni raviṃ kapiḥ
Bhk dīpitāraṃ dinā''rambhe nirastadhvāntasaṃcayam
Bhk atīte varṣuke kāle
pramattaḥ sthāyuko gṛhe
Bhk gāmuko dhruvamadhvānaṃ sugrīvo vālinā gatam
Bhk jalpākībhiḥ sahā ''sīnaḥ strībhiḥ prajavinā tvayā
Bhk gatvā lakṣmaṇa 
vaktavyo jayinā niṣṭhuraṃ vacaḥ
Bhk śaile viśrayiṇaṃ kṣipramanādariṇamabhyamī

Bhk viduro jitvaraḥ prāpa lakṣmaṇo gatvarān kapīn

Bhk ahaṃ svapnak prasādena tava vandārubhiḥ saha

Bhk eṣa śokacchido vīrān prabho 
samprati vānarān

atha niradhikārakṛt
Bhk rāghavasya tataḥ kāryaṃ kārur vānarapuṅgavaḥ
Bhk sarvavānarasenānāmāśvāgamanamādiśat

Bhk tataḥ kapīnāṃ saṃghātā harṣād rāghavabhūtaye

Bhk kākutsthapādapacchāyāṃ sītasparśāmupāgamat

tat kāryaṃ paryāyeṇā 'virodhibhiḥ

suṣeṇaṃ pakṣimāṃ tathā

yatnenā ''khyāyatāṃ śubhe

kīrtiṃ vā pātumātmanaḥ

Bhk niṣkramya śikṣayā tasyās trapāvanto rasātalāt

Bhk jaṭāyuḥ puṇyakṛt pakṣī daṇḍakāraṇyasañcaraḥ

atha prakīrṇakāḥ
Bhk ātmanaḥ paridevadhve kurvanto rāmasaṃkathām

na gacchāmaḥ kauśalyāyanivallabhām

Bhk uditvā 'laṃ ciraṃ yatnāt saikā dhātrā vinirmitā

kṛṣīḍhvaṃ svāmine hitaṃ

dhairyaṃ cā''dhiṣatā 'dhikam

Bhk āgādhata tato vyoma hanūmānuruvigrahaḥ
Bhk atyaśerata tadvegaṃ na suparṇā'rkamārutāḥ
Bhk abhāyata yathā'rkeṇa suprātena śaranmukhe

Bhk vyatijigye samudro'pi na dhairyaṃ tasya gacchataḥ

Bhk jaghānā''viśya vadanaṃ niryāt bhittvodaraṃ drutam
Bhk anyonyaṃ sma vyatiyutaḥ śabdān śabdais tu bhīṣaṇān
Bhk udanvāṃś cāniloddhūto mriyamāṇā ca rākṣasī

parikrīḍasva sānuṣu

Bhk kṣaṇaṃ bhadrā'vatiṣṭhasva
tataḥ prasthāsyase punaḥ
Bhk na tat saṃsthāsyate kāryaṃ dakṣeṇorīkṛtaṃ tvayā

vāyorahaṃ suhṛt

 mā kasyacidupaskṛthāḥ

kenacid vyavadiṣṭa na

nā 'śuśrūṣata gāyanān

Bhk śatasāhasramārakṣaṃ madhyagaṃ rakṣasāṃ kapiḥ
Bhk dadarśa yaṃ kṛtānto'pi mriyetā''sādya bhīṣaṇam
Bhk adhyāsisiṣamāṇe 'tha viyanmadhyaṃ niśākare
Bhk kāsāṃcakre purī saughairatīvodbhāsibhiḥ sitaiḥ
Bhk induṃ caṣakasaṃkrāntamupāyuṅkta yathā'mṛtam
Bhk payuñjānaḥ priyā vācaḥ samājā'nurato janaḥ
Bhk saṃkṣṇuvāna ivotkaṇṭhāmupābhuṅkta surāmalam
Bhk jyotsnāyāṃ vigalanmānas taruṇo rakṣasāṃ gaṇaḥ
Bhk madhvapāyayata svacchaṃ sotpalaṃ dayitā'ntike
Bhk ātmānaṃ suratā''bhogaviśrambhotpādanaṃ muhuḥ
Bhk abhīṣayanta ye śakraṃ rākṣasā raṇapaṇḍitāḥ
Bhk avismāpayamānas tān kapiroṭīd gṛhād gṛham
Bhk sītāṃ didṛkṣuḥ pracchannaḥ so 'gardhayata rākṣasān
Bhk avañcayata māyāś ca svamāyābhir naradviṣām
Bhk apalāpayamānasya śatrūṃs tasyā'bhavan matiḥ
Bhk mithyā kārayate cārair ghoṣaṇāṃ rākṣasā'dhipaḥ
Bhk gūhamānaḥ svamāhātmyamaṭitvā mantrisaṃsadaḥ
Bhk nṛbhyo 'pavadamānasya rāvaṇasya gṛhaṃ yayau
Bhk diśo dyotayamānābhir divyanārībhirākulam
Bhk śriyamāyacchamānābhiruttamābhiranuttamām
Bhk nityamudyacchamānābhiḥ smarasaṃbhogakarmasu
Bhk jānānābhiralaṃ līlākila kiṃcitavibhramān
Bhk svaṃ karma kārayannāste niścinto yā jhaṣadhvajaḥ
Bhk svārthaṃ kārayamāṇābhir yūno madavimohitān
Bhk kāntiṃ svāṃ vahamānābhir yajantībhiḥ svavigrahān

Bhk tā hanūmān parākurvannagamat puṣpakaṃ prati

Bhk kṣaṇaṃ paryaramat tasya darśanān mārutā''tmajaḥ
Bhk upāraṃsīc ca saṃpaśyan vānaras taṃ cikīrṣitāt
Bhk ramyaṃ merumivā''dhūtakānanaṃ śvasanormibhiḥ

Bhk tataḥ prākāramārohat kṣapāṭānavibodhayan
Bhk nā'yodhayat samartho'pi sītādarśanalālasaḥ
Bhk adhyāsīd
rāghavasyā 'haṃ nāśayeyaṃ kathaṃ śucam
Bhk vaidehyā janayeyaṃ vā kathamānandamuttamam
Bhk dṛṣṭvā rāghavakāntāṃ tāṃ drāvayiṣyāmi rākṣasān
Bhk tasyā hi darśanāt pūrvaṃ vikramaḥ kāryanāśakṛt
Bhk cintayannitthamuttuṅgaiḥ prāvayantīṃ divaṃ vanaiḥ
Bhk aśokavanikāmārādapaśyat stabakā''citām

Bhk nā''yāsayanta saṃtrastā ṛtavo'nyonyasaṃpadaḥ
Bhk jyotsnā 'mṛtaṃ śaśī vasyāṃ vāpīr vikasitotpalāḥ
Bhk apāyayata saṃpūrṇaḥ sadā daśamukhā''jñayā
Bhk prādamayanta puṣpeṣuṃ yasyāṃ bandyaḥ samāhṛtāḥ
Bhk parimohayamāṇābhī rākṣasībhiḥ samāvṛtāḥ
Bhk yasyāṃ vāsayate sītāṃ kevalaṃ sma ripuḥ smarāt
Bhk na tvarocayatā ''tmānaṃ caturo vṛddhimānapi

vyarucan kumudā''karāḥ

vitathaiva naḥ

Bhk tāṃ parājayamānāṃ sa prīte rakṣyāṃ daśā''nanāt

Bhk rāmādadhītasaṃdeśo vāyor jātaś cyutasmitām

Bhk ślāghamānaḥ parastrībhyas tatra''gād rākṣasā'dhipaḥ
Bhk aśapta nihnuvāno 'sau sītāyau smaramohitaḥ
Bhk dhārayānniva caitasyai vasūni pratyapadyata

Bhk sānunītiś ca sītāyai na 'krudhyan
nāpyasūyata
Bhk saṃkrudhyasi mṛśā kiṃ tvaṃ didṛkṣuṃ māṃ mṛgekṣaṇe 
Bhk īkṣitavyaṃ parastrībhyaḥ svadharmo rakṣasāmayam
Bhk śṛṇvadbhyaḥ pratiśṛṇvanti madhyamā bhīru  nottamāḥ
Bhk gṛṇadbhyo 'nugṛṇantyanye 'kṛtā'rthā
naiva madvidhāḥ
Bhk iccha snehena dīvyantī viṣayān bhuvaneśvaram
Bhk saṃbhogāya parikrītaḥ kartāsmi tava nā 'priyam
Bhk āssva sākaṃ mayā saudhe
mā'dhiṣṭhā nirjanaṃ vanam
Bhk mā 'dhivātsīr bhuvaṃ
śayyāmadhiśeṣva smarotsukā
Bhk abhinyavikṣathās tvaṃ me yathaivā'vyāhatā manaḥ
Bhk tavā'pyadhyāvasantaṃ māṃ mā rautsīr hṛdayaṃ tathā
Bhk mā 'vamaṃsthā nāmasyantamkāryajñe 
jagatpatim
Bhk saṃdṛṣṭe mayi kākutsthamadhanyaṃ kāmayeta  kā
Bhk yaḥ payo dogdhi pāṣāṇaṃ
sa rāmād bhūtimāpnuyāt
Bhk rāvaṇaṃ gamaya prītiṃ bodhayantaṃ hitā'hitaṃ
Bhk prīto 'haṃ bhojayiṣyāmi bhavatīṃ bhuvanatrayam
Bhk kiṃ vilāpayase'tyarthaṃ
pārśve śāyaya rāvaṇam
Bhk ājñāṃ kāraya rakṣobhir
mā priyāṇyupahāraya
Bhk kaḥ śakreṇa kṛtaṃ necchedadhimurdhānamañjalim
iti kārakādhikāraḥ
Bhk vacanaṃ rakṣasāṃ patyuranu kruddhā patipriyā

Bhk na bhavānanu rāmaṃ cedupa śūreṣu vā tataḥ
Bhk apavāhya cchalād vīrau kimarthaṃ māmihā 'haraḥ
Bhk upaśūraṃ na te vṛttaṃ kathaṃ rātriṃcarā'dhama 
Bhk yat saṃpratyapalokebhyo laṅkāyāṃ vasatir bhayāt

vidyotasva striyaḥ prati

Bhk kuto 'dhiyāsyasi krūra 
nihatas tena patribhiḥ

bhavato grahaṇaṃ kiyat

mayyapi yo 'bhikaḥ

Bhk tataḥ khaḍgaṃ samudyamya rāvaṇaḥ krūravigrahaḥ
Bhk vaidehīmantarā kruddhaḥ kṣaṇamūce viniśvasan
Bhk cireṇā 'nuguṇaṃ proktā pratipattiparāṅmukhī

martāsi maithili 
Bhk prāyuṅkta rākṣasīr bhīmā mandirāya prativrajan

Bhk gate tasmin samājagmur bhayāya prati maithilīm

rāvaṇaprītyai krūraṃ cocuralaṃ muhuḥ

svamāṃsaiḥ kurutā 'śanam

Bhk atha lulitapatatrimālaṃ rugṇā'sanabāṇakeśaratamālam
Bhk sa vanaṃ viviktamālaṃ sītāṃ draṣṭuṃ jagāmā'lam
Bhk ghanagirīndravilaṅghanaśālinā vanagatā vanajadyutilocanā
Bhk janamatā dadṛśe janakā''tmajā tarumṛgeṇa tarusthalaśāyinī
vipathayamakam
Bhk kāntā mahamānā duḥkhaṃ cyutabhūṣā
Bhk rāmasya viyuktā kāntā sahamānā
madhyā'ntayamakam
Bhk mitamavadadudāraṃ tāṃ hanūmān mudā 'raṃ raghuvṛṣabhasakāśaṃ yāmi devi  prakāśam
Bhk tava viditaviṣādo dṛṣṭakṛtsnā''miṣādaḥ śriyamaniśamavantaṃ parvataṃ mālyavantam
garbhayamakam
Bhk udapatad viyadapragamaḥ parai rucitamunnatimatpṛthusattvavat
Bhk rucitamun natimat pṛthusattvavat pratividhāya vaṇur bhayadaṃ dviṣām
sarvayamakam
Bhk babhau marutvān vikṛtaḥ samudro
babhau marutvān vikṛtaḥ samudraḥ
Bhk babhau marutvān vikṛtaḥ samudro
babhau marutvān vikṛtaḥ sa mudraḥ
mahāyamakam
Bhk abhiyātā varaṃ tuṅgaṃ bhūbhṛtaṃ ruciraṃ puraḥ karkaśaṃ prathitaṃ dhāma sasatvaṃ puṣkarekṣaṇam
Bhk abhiyā 'tā''varaṃ tuṅgaṃ bhūbhṛtaṃ ruciraṃ puraḥ karkaśaṃ prasthitaṃ dhāma sasatvaṃ puṣkare kṣaṇam
ādyantayamakam
Bhk citraṃ citramivā ''yāto vicitraṃ tasya bhūbhṛtam
Bhk harayo vegamāsādya saṃtrastā mumuhur muhuḥ
ādidīpakam
Bhk gacchan sa vārīṇyakirat pāyodheḥ
kūlasthitāṃs tānitarūnadhunvan
Bhk puṣpā''starāṃs te 'ṅgasūkhānatanvan
tān kinnarā manmathino 'dhyatiṣṭhan
antadīpakam
Bhk sa giriṃ tarukhaṇḍamaṇḍitaṃ samavāpya tvarayā latāmṛgaḥ
Bhk smitadarśitakāryaniścayaḥ kapisainyair muditairamaṇḍayat
madhyadīpakam
Bhk garuḍā'nilatigmaraśmayaḥ patatāṃ yadhapi saṃmatā jave
Bhk acireṇa kṛtā'rthamāgataṃ tamamanyanta tathāpyatīva te
rūpakam
Bhk vraṇakandaralīnaśastrasarpaḥ pṛthuvakṣaḥsthalakarkaśorubhittiḥ
Bhk cyutaśoṇitabaddhadhāturāgaḥ śuśubhe vānarabhūdharas tadā 'sau
asyaiva bhedā apare catvāraḥ etad viśiṣṭopamāyuktaṃ rūpakam
Bhk calapiṅgakeśarahiraṇyalatāḥ sthuṭanetrapaṅktimaṇisaṃhatayaḥ
Bhk kaladhaitasānava ivā 'tha gireḥ kapayo bahūḥ pavanajā''gamane
etaccheṣā'rthā'nvavasitamavataṃsakam
Bhk kapitoyanidhīn plavaṅgamendur madayitvā madhureṇa darśanena
Bhk vacanā'mṛtadīdhitīr vitanva nnakṛtā ''nandaparītanetravārīn
ardharūpakam
Bhk parikheditavindhyavīrudhaḥ paripītā'malanirjharā'mbhasaḥ
Bhk dudhuvur madhukānanaṃ tataḥ kapināgā muditā'ṅgadā''jñayā
etadanvarthopamāyuktaṃ lalāmakam
Bhk viṭapimṛgaviṣādadhvāntanud vānarā'rkaḥ priyavacanamayukhair bodhitā'rthā'ravindaḥ
Bhk udayagirimivā 'driṃ saṃpramucyā 'bhyagāt khaṃ nṛpahṛdayaguhākhaṃ ghnan pramohā'ndhakāram
ivopamā
Bhk raghutanayamagāt tapovanakhaṃ vidhṛtajaṭā'jinavalkalaṃ hanūmān
Bhk paramiva puruṣaṃ nareṇa yuktaṃ samaśamaveśasamādhinā 'nujena
yathopamā
Bhk karapuṭanihitaṃ dadhat sa ratnaṃ pariviralā'ṅguli nirgatā'lpadīpti
Bhk tanukapilaghanasthitaṃ yathenduṃ nṛpamanamat paribhugnajānumūrdhā
sahopamā
Bhk rucironnataratnagauravaḥ paripūrṇā'mṛtaraśmimaṇḍalaḥ
Bhk samadṛśyata jīvitā''śayā saha rāmeṇa vadhūśiromaṇiḥ
taddhitopamā
Bhk avasannaruciṃ vanā''gataṃ tamanā''mṛṣṭarajovidhūsaram
Bhk samapaśyadapetamaithiliṃ dadhataṃ gauravamātramātmavat
luptopamā
Bhk sāmarthyasaṃpāditavāñchitā'rthaś cintāmaṇiḥ syān na kathaṃ hanūmān
Bhk salakṣmaṇo bhūmipatis tadānīṃ śākhāmṛgā'nīkapatiś ca mene
samopamā
Bhk yuśmānacetan kṣayavāyukalpān sītāsphuliṅgaṃ parigṛhya jālmaḥ
Bhk laṅkāvanaṃ siṃhasamo 'dhiśete martuṃ dviṣannityavadaddhanūmān
arthā'ntaranyāsaḥ
Bhk ahṛta dhaneśvarasya yudhi yaḥ sametamāyo dhanaṃ
tamahamito vilokya vibudhaiḥ kṛtottamā''yodhanam

ākṣepaḥ
Bhk ṛddhimān rākṣaso mūḍhaś
citraṃ nā'sau yaddudhataḥ
Bhk ko vā heturanāryāṇāṃ dharmye vartmani vartitum
ākṣepa eva
Bhk tasyā 'dhivāse tanurutsukā 'sau dṛṣṭā mayā rāmapatiḥ pramanyuḥ
Bhk kāryasya sāro 'yamudīrito vaḥ
proktena śeṣeṇa kimuddhatena
vyatirekaḥ
Bhk samatāṃ śaśilekhayopayāyā davadātā pratanuḥ kṣayeṇa sītā
Bhk yadi nāma kalaṅka indulekhā mativṛtto laghayen na cā 'pi bhāvī
vibhāvanā
Bhk aparīkṣitakāriṇā gṛhītāṃ tvamanāsevitavṛddhapaṇḍitena
Bhk avirodhitaniṣṭhureṇa sādhvīṃ dayitāṃ trātumalaṃ ghaṭasva rājan 
samāsoktiḥ
Bhk sa ca vihvalasattvasaṃkulaḥ pariśuṣyannabhavan mahāhradaḥ
Bhk paritaḥ paritāpamūrcchitaḥ
patitaṃ cā 'mbu nirabhramīpsitam
atiśayoktiḥ
Bhk atha lakṣmaṇatulyarūpaveśaṃ gamanā''deśavinirgatā'grahastam
Bhk kapayo 'nuyayuḥ sametya rāmaṃ natasugrīvagṛhītasā''darājñam
yathāsaṃkhyam
Bhk kapipṛṣṭhagatau tato narendrau kapayaś ca jvalitā'gnipiṅgalā'kṣāḥ
Bhk mumucuḥ prayayur
drutaṃ samīyur
vasudhāṃ
vyoma

utprekṣā
Bhk sthitamiva parirakṣituṃ samantā dudadhijalaughapariplavād dharitrīm
Bhk gaganatalavasundhrā'ntarāle jalanidhivegasahaṃ prasārya deham
vārtā
Bhk viṣadharanilaye niviṣṭamūlaṃ śikharaśataiḥ parimṛṣṭadevalokam
Bhk ghanavipulanitambapūritāśaṃ phalakusumā''citavṛkṣaramyakuñjam
preyaḥ
Bhk madhukaravirutaiḥ priyādhvanīnāṃ sarasiruhair dayitā''syahāsyalakṣmyāḥ
Bhk sphuṭamanuharamāṇamādadhānaṃ puruṣapateḥ sahasā paraṃpramodam
rasavat
Bhk grahamaṇirasanaṃ divo nitambaṃ vipulamanuttamalabdhakāntiyogam
Bhk cyutaghanavasanaṃ mano'bhirāmaṃ śikharakarair madanādiva spṛśantam
ūrjasvī
Bhk pracapalamaguruṃ bharā'sahiṣṇuṃ janamasamānamanūrjitaṃ vivarjya
Bhk kṛtavasatimivā'rṇavopakaṇṭhe sthiramatulonnatimūḍhatuṅgamegham
paryāyoktiḥ
Bhk sphaṭhikamaṇigṛhaiḥ saratnadīpaiḥ prataruṇakinnaragītanisvanaiś ca

samāhitam
Bhk atha dadṛśurudīrṇadhūmadhūmrāṃ diśamudadhivyavadhiṃ sametasītām
Bhk saharaghutanayāḥ plavaṅgasenāḥ pavanasutā'ṅgulidarśitāmudakṣāḥ
udāram
Bhk jalanidhimagaman mahendrakuñjāt pracayatirohitatigmaraśmibhāsaḥ

udārameva
Bhk pṛthugurumaṇiśuktigarbhabhāsā glapitarasātalasaṃbhṛtā'ndhakāram
Bhk upahataraviraśmivṛttimuccaiḥ pralaghupariplavamānavajrajālaiḥ
udārameva
Bhk samupacitajalaṃ vivardhamānai ramalasaritsalilair vibhāvarīṣu

śliṣṭam

śliṣṭameva
Bhk pradadṛśururumuktaśīkaraughān vimalamaṇidyutisaṃbhṛtendracāpān

hetuśliṣṭam

apahnutiḥ

viśeṣoktiḥ

vyājastutiḥ

Bhk giriparigatacañcalā''pagā'ntaṃ jalanivahaṃ dadhataṃ mano'bhirāmam

virodhaḥ

na ca madanaḥ kṣatamātatān nā 'rciḥ
upameyopamā

sahoktiḥ
Bhk apaharadiva sarvato vinodān dayitagataṃ dadhadekadhā samādhim

Bhk vidadhadiva jagat punaḥ pralīnam bhavati mahān hi parā'rtha eva sarvaḥ
sasandehaḥ
Bhk aśanirayamasau
kuto nirabhre śitaśaravarṣamasat tadapyaśārṅgam

na ca niścikāya candram
ananvayaḥ
Bhk kumudavanacayeṣu kīrṇaraśmiḥ kṣatatimireśu ca digvadhūmukheṣu

vilasati candramaso na yadvadanyaḥ
utprekṣā''vayavaḥ
Bhk śaraṇamiva gataṃ tamo nikuñje viṭapinirākṛtacandraraśmyarātau

saṃsṛṣṭiḥ

Bhk raghusutamanujo jagāda vācaṃ sajalaghanastanayitnutulyaghoṣaḥ

jahīhi śokaṃ

hetuḥ
Bhk adhigatamahimā manuśyaloke vata sutarāmavasīdati pramādī
Bhk gajapatiruruśailaśṛṅgavarṣmā gururavamajjati paṅkabhāṅ na dāru
nipuṇam
Bhk boddhavyaṃ kimiva hi
yat tvayā na buddhaṃ
kiṃ vā te nimiṣitamapyabuddhipūrvam
Bhk labdhā''tmā tava sukṛtairaniṣṭaśaṅkī snehaugho ghaṭayati māṃ tathāpi vaktum
Bhk saumitreriti vacanaṃ niśamya rāmo jṛmbhāvān bhujayugalaṃ vibhajya nidrān
Bhk adhyaṣṭhāc chiśayiṣayā pravālatalpaṃ rakṣāyai pratidiśamādiśan plavaṅgān
Bhk athā 'stamāseduṣi mandakāntau puṇyakṣayeṇeva nidhau kalānām
Bhk samālalambe ripumitrakalpaiḥ padmaiḥ prahāsaḥ kumudair viṣādaḥ
Bhk dūraṃ samāruhya divaḥ patantaṃ bhṛgorivenduṃ vihitopakāram
Bhk baddhā 'nurāgo 'nupapāta tūrṇaṃ tārāgaṇaḥ saṃbhṛtaśubhrakīrtiḥ
Bhk kva te kaṭākṣāḥ
kva vilāsavanti proktāni vā tāni mameti matvā
Bhk laṅkā'ṅganānāmavabodhakāle lulāmanāruhya gato 'staminduḥ
Bhk mānena talpeṣvayathāmukhīnā mithyāprasuptair gamitatriyāmāḥ
Bhk strībhir niśā'tikramavihvalābhir dṛṣṭe 'pi doṣe patayo 'nunītāḥ
Bhk īrśyāvirugṇāḥ sthirabaddhamūlā nirastaniḥśeṣaśubhapratānāḥ
Bhk āpyāyitā netrajalaprasekaiḥ premadrumāḥ saṃruruhuḥ priyāṇām
Bhk tataḥ samāśaṅkitaviprayogaḥ punarnavībhūtaraso 'vitṛṣṇaḥ
Bhk smarasya santaṃ punaruktabhāvaṃ nā ''vartamānasya viveda lokaḥ
Bhk vṛttau prakāśaṃ hṛdaye kṛtāyāṃ sukhena sarvendriyasaṃbhavena
Bhk saṃkocamevā 'sahamānamasthā daśaktavad vañcitamāni cakṣuḥ
Bhk pīne bhaṭasyorasi vīkṣya bhugnāṃs tanutvacaḥ pāṇiruhān sumadhyā
Bhk icchāvibhaṅgā''kulamānasatvād bhartre nakhebhyaś ca ciraṃ jujūre
Bhk srastā'ṅgaceṣṭo vinimīlitā'kṣaḥ svedā'mburomodgamagamyajīvaḥ

sukhaṃ nu
mūrcchā nu

Bhk vakṣaḥ stanābhyāṃ
sukhamānanena gātrāṇi gātrair ghaṭayannamandam

paryāptatā premṇi kuto viruddhā

Bhk anūḍhamānā śayane navoḍhā paropakāraikarasaiva tasthau

Bhk pranaṣṭamūrtipravibhāgamudyan pratyujjahāreva tato vivasvān

Bhk prajāgarā''tāmravilocanā'ntā nirañjanā'laktakapatralekhāḥ
Bhk tulyā ivā ''san parikhedatanvyo vāsacyutāḥ sevitamanmathābhiḥ
Bhk ābaddhanetrā'ñjanapaṅkaleśas tāmbūlarāgaṃ bahulaṃ dadhānaḥ

Bhk kurvan savāsaṃ ca sugandhi vaktraṃ cakre janaḥ kevalapakṣapātam
Bhk kṣatairasaṃcetitadantalabdhaiḥ saṃbhogakāle 'vagataiḥ prabhāte
Bhk aśaṅkatā 'nyonyakṛtaṃ vyalīkaṃ viyogabāhyo 'pi jano 'tirāgāt
Bhk netreṣubhiḥ saṃyutapakṣmapatraiḥ karṇā'ntakṛṣṭairurukeśaśūlāḥ
Bhk stanorucakrās tatakarṇapāśāḥ strīyoddhamukhyā jayino viceruḥ
Bhk payodharāṃś candanapaṅkadigdhān vāsāṃsi cā 'mṛṣṭamṛjāni dṛṣṭvā

Bhk smarā''ture cetasi labdhajanmā rarāja lolo'pi guṇā'pahāryaḥ
Bhk kutūhalān netragavākṣasaṃsthaḥ paśyannivā 'nyonyamukhāni rāgaḥ
Bhk gate 'tibhūmiṃ praṇaye prayuktā nabuddhipūrvaṃ pariluptasaṃjñaḥ
Bhk ātmā'nubhūtānapi nopacārān smarā''turaḥ saṃsmarati sma lokaḥ
Bhk vastrairanatyulbaṇaramyavarṇair vilepanaiḥ saurabhalakṣmaṇīyaiḥ
Bhk āsyaiś ca lokaḥ paritoṣakāntai rasūcayal labdhapadaṃ rahasyam
Bhk prātastarāṃ candanaliptagātrāḥ pracchādya hastairadharān vadantaḥ

kimudyataṃ bhrūdhanurprasahyam
Bhk hantuṃ kṣamo vā vada locaneṣur digdho viṣeṇeva kimañjanena
Bhk dantacchade prajvalitā'gnikalpe tāmbūlarāgas tṛṇabhāratulyaḥ
Bhk nyastaḥ kimityūcurupetabhāvā goṣṭhīṣu nārīs taruṇīr yuvānaḥ
Bhk sukhā'vagāhāni yutāni lakṣmyā śucīni saṃtāpaharāṇyurūṇi
Bhk prabuddhanārīmukhapaṅkajāni prātaḥ sarāṃsīva gṛhāṇi rejuḥ
Bhk saṃmṛṣṭasiktā'rcitacārupuṣpai rāmodavaddravyasugandhabhāgaiḥ
Bhk lakṣmīr vijigye bhavanaiḥ sabhṛṅgaiḥ sevyasya devairapi nandanasya
Bhk akṣṇoḥ patan nīlasarojalobhād bhṛṅgaḥ kareṇā 'lpadhiyā nirastaḥ
Bhk dadaṃśa tāmrā'mburuhā'bhisandhis trṇā''turaḥ pāṇitale 'pi dhṛṣṇuḥ
Bhk vilolatāṃ cakṣuṣi hastavepathuṃ bhruvor vibhaṅgaṃ stanayugmavalgitam
Bhk vibhūṣaṇānāṃ kvaṇitaṃ ca ṣaṭpado gurur yathā nṛtyavidhau samādadhe
Bhk athā 'nukūlān kuladharmasaṃpado vidhāya veśān sudivaḥ purījanaḥ
Bhk prabodhakāle śātamanyuvidviṣaḥ pracakrame rājaniketanaṃ prati
Bhk śailendraśṛṅgebhya iva pravṛttā vegāj jalaughāḥ puramandirebhyaḥ
Bhk āpūrya rathyāḥ sarito janaughā rājā'ṅganā'mbhodhimapūrayanta
Bhk prabodhakālāt tridaśendraśatroḥ prāgūrdhvaśoṣaṃ pariśuṣyamāṇāḥ
Bhk hīnā mahāntaś ca samatvamīyur dvāsasthairavajñāpuruṣā'kṣidṛṣtāḥ
Bhk gurūrucañcatkarakarṇajihvai ravajñayā 'grā'ṅgulisaṃgṛhītaiḥ
Bhk rakṣāmsyanāyāsahṛtairupāsthuḥ kapolalīnā'likulair gajendraiḥ
Bhk nikṛttamattadvipakumbhamāṃsaiḥ saṃpṛktamuktair harayo'grapādaiḥ
Bhk āninyire śreṇikṛtās tathā 'nyaiḥ parasparaṃ vāladhisannibaddhāḥ
Bhk upekṣitā devagaṇais trasadbhir niṣācarair vītabhayair nikṛttāḥ
Bhk tasminnadṛśyanta suradrumāṇāṃ sajālapuṣpastabakāḥ prakīrṇāḥ
Bhk nirākariṣṇur dvijakuñjarāṇāṃ tṛṇīkṛtā'śeṣaguṇo'timohāt
Bhk pāpā'śayānabhyudayā'rthamārcīt prāg brahmarakṣaḥpravarān daśā''syaḥ
Bhk māyāvibhis trāsakarair janānā māptairupādānaparairupetaḥ
Bhk satāṃ vighātaikarasairavikṣat sadaḥ parikṣobhitabhūmibhāgam
Bhk vighṛtaniśitaśastrais tad yutaṃ yātudhānai rurujaṭharamukhībhiḥ saṃkulaṃ rākṣasībhiḥ
Bhk śvagaṇiśatavikīrṇaṃ vāgurāvan mṛgībhir vanamiva sabhayābhir devabandībhirāsīt
Bhk jalada iva taḍitvān prājyaratnaprabhābhiḥ pratikakubhamudasyan nisvanaṃ dhīramandram
Bhk śikharamiva sumerorāsanaṃ haimamuccair vividhamaṇivicitraṃ pronnataṃ so 'dhyatiṣthat
Bhk tato vinidraṃ kṛtadevatā'rcaṃ dṛṣṭyaiva cittapraśamaṃ kirantam
Bhk āviṣkṛtā'ṅgapratikarmaramyaṃ vibhīṣaṇaṃ vācamuvāca mātā
Bhk prabādhamānasya jaganti dhīmaṃs 
tvaṃ sodarasyā'timadoddhatasya
Bhk ānandano nākasadāṃ praśāntiṃ tūrṇaṃ viṣasyā'mṛtavat kuruṣva
Bhk kuryās tathā
yena jahāti sītāṃ viṣādanīhāraparītamūrtim
Bhk sthitāṃ kṣitau śāntaśikhāpratānāṃ tārāmiva trāsakarīṃ janasya
Bhk yāvan na saṃtrāsitadevasaṃghaḥ piṇḍo viṣasyeva hareṇa bhīṣmaḥ
Bhk saṃgrasyate 'sau puruṣā'dhipena
drutaṃ kulā''nanda 
yatasva tāvat
Bhk hatā janasthāna sado nikāyāḥ
kṛtā jitotkhātabhaṭadrumā pūḥ
Bhk sadāṃsi dagdhāni
vidheyamasmin yad bandhunā
tad ghaṭayasva tasmin
Bhk cikīrṣite pūrvataraṃ sa tasmin
kṣemaṃkare 'rthe muhurīryamāṇaḥ
Bhk mātrā 'timātraṃ śubhayaiva buddhyā ciraṃ sudhīrabhyadhikaṃ samādhāt
Bhk dauvārikā'bhyāhataśakradūtaṃ sopāyanopasthitalokapālam
Bhk sā''śaṅkabhīṣmā''ptaviśanniśāṭaṃ dvāraṃ yayau rāvaṇamandrirasya
Bhk dūrāt pratīhāranataḥ sa vārtāṃ pṛcchannanāveditasaṃpraviṣṭaḥ
Bhk sagauravaṃ dattapatho niśāṭai raikṣiṣṭa śailā'gramivendraśatrum
Bhk kṛśānuvarṣmaṇyadhirūḍhamuccaiḥ siṃhāsane saṃkṣayameghabhīmam
Bhk nisargatīkṣṇaṃ nayanasphuliṅgaṃ yugāntavahneriva dhūmarāśim
Bhk prītyā 'pi dattekṣaṇasannipātaṃ bhayaṃ bhūjaṅgā'dhipavad dadhānam
Bhk tamaḥsamūhā''kṛtimapyaśeṣā nūrjā jayantaṃ prathitaprakāśān
Bhk taṃ ratnadāyaṃ jitamṛtyulokā rātriṃcarāḥ kāntibhṛto 'nvasarpan
Bhk pramuktamuktāphalamambuvāhaṃ saṃjātatṛṣṇā iva devamukhyāḥ
Bhk sa kiṅkaraiḥ kalpitamiṅgitajñaiḥ saṃbādhakaṃ pūrvasamāgatānām
Bhk siṃhāsanopāśritacārubāhu radhyāsta pīṭhaṃ vihitapraṇāmaḥ
Bhk tato daśā''syaḥ kṣubhitā'hikalpaṃ dīprā'ṅgulīyopalamūḍharatnam
Bhk anekacañcannakhakāntijihvaṃ prasārya pāṇiṃ samitiṃ babhāṣe
Bhk śaktaiḥ suhṛdbhiḥ paridṛṣṭakāryai rāmnātibhir nītiṣu buddhimadbhiḥ
Bhk yuṣmadvidhaiḥ sārdhamupāyavidbhiḥ sadhyanti kāryāṇi sumantritāni
Bhk upekṣite vālikharā''dināśe
dagdhe pure
'kṣe nihate sabhṛtye
Bhk sainye dviṣāṃ sāgaramuttitīrṣā vanantaraṃ brūta
yadatra yuktam
Bhk bhujāṃ'savakṣaḥsthalakārmukā'sīn gadāś ca śūlāni ca yātudhānāḥ
Bhk parāmṛśantaḥ prathitā'bhimānāḥ procuḥ prahastapramukhā daśā''syam
Bhk akhaṇḍyamānaṃ parikhaṇḍya śakraṃ tvaṃ paṇḍitaṃmanyamudīrṇadaṇḍaḥ
Bhk narā''bhiyogaṃ nṛbhujāṃ pradhāna 
mantronmukhaḥ kiṃ nayase gurutvam
Bhk niryatsphuliṅgā''kuladhūmarāśiṃ kiṃ brūhi bhūmau pinaṣāma bhānum
Bhk ā dantaniṣpīḍitapītaminduṃ ṣṭhīvāma śuṣkekṣulatā'sthikalpam
Bhk sarāghavaiḥ kiṃ bata vānarais tair yaiḥ prātarāśo 'pi na kasyacin naḥ
Bhk sasthāṇukailāsadhāra 'bhidhatsva
kiṃ dyauradho 'stu
kṣitirantarīkṣe
Bhk cāpalyayuktasya hareḥ kṛśānuḥ samedhito vāladhibhāk tvadīyaiḥ
Bhk śastreṇa vadhyasya galannadhākṣīd rājan 
pramādena nijena laṅkām
Bhk athā 'ñcitoraskamudīrṇadṛṣṭiḥ kṛtvā vivakṣāpravaṇaṃ śarīram
Bhk vivṛttapāṇir vihitottarā'rthaṃ vibhīṣaṇo 'bhāṣata yātudhānān
Bhk yuddhāya rājṇā subhṛtair bhavadbhiḥ saṃbhāvanāyāḥ sadṛśaṃ yaduktam
Bhk tat prāṇapaṇyair vacanīyameva
prajñā tu mantre 'dhikṛtā na śauryam
Bhk yac cāpi yatnā''dṛtamantravṛttir gurutvamāyāti narā'bhiyogaḥ
Bhk vaśīkṛtendrasya
kṛtottaro 'smin vidhvaṃsitā'śeṣapuro hanūmān
Bhk agniḥ pramādena dadāha laṅkāṃ vadhyasya dehe svayamedhitaś cet
Bhk vimṛśya tad devadhiyā 'bhidhatta brahmā'strabandho'pi yadi pramādaḥ
Bhk jagantyameyā'dbhutabhāvabhāñji
jitā'bhimānāś ca janā vicitrāḥ
Bhk kārye tu yatnaṃ kuruta prakṛṣṭaṃ
mā nītigarbhān sudhiyo 'vamandhvam
Bhk vṛddhikṣayasthānagatāmajasraṃ vṛttiṃ jigīṣuḥ prasamīkṣamāṇaḥ
Bhk ghaṭeta sandhyā''diṣu yo guṇeṣu
lakṣmīr na taṃ muñcati cañcalā 'pi
Bhk upekṣaṇīyaiva parasya vṛddhiḥ pranaṣṭanīterajitendrayasya
Bhk madā''diyuktasya virāgahetuḥ
samūlaghātaṃ vinihanti yā 'nte
Bhk janā'nurāgeṇa yuto 'vasādaḥ phalā'nubandhaḥ sudhiyā ''tmano 'pi
Bhk upekṣaṇīyo 'bhyupagamya saṃdhiṃ kāmā''diṣaḍvargajitā 'dhipena
Bhk yadā vigṛhṇan na ca saṃdadhāno vṛddhiṃ kṣayaṃ cā 'nuguṇaṃ prapaśyet
Bhk āsīta rājā 'vasarapratīkṣas tadā prayāsaṃ vitathaṃ na kuryāt
Bhk saṃdhau sthito vā janayet svavṛddhiṃ hanyāt paraṃ vopaniṣatprayogaiḥ
Bhk āśrāvayedasya janaṃ parair vā vigrāhya kuryādavahīnasaṃdhim
Bhk saṃdarśitasnehaguṇaḥ svaśatrūn vidveṣayan maṇḍalamasya bhindyāt
Bhk ityevamādi pravidhāya saṃdhir vṛddher vidheyo 'dhigamābhyupāyaḥ
Bhk matvā sahiṣṇūnaparopajapyān svakānadhiṣṭhāya jalā'ntadurgān
Bhk drumā'dridurlaṅghyajalāpradhṛṣyān vardheta rājā ripuvigraheṇa
Bhk śaknoti yo na dviṣato nihantuṃ
vihanyate nā 'pyabalair dviṣadbhiḥ
Bhk sa śvāvarāhaṃ kalahaṃ vidadhyā dāsīta durgā''di vivardhayaṃś ca
Bhk prayāṇamātreṇa pare prasādye varteta yānena kṛtā'bhirakṣaḥ
Bhk aśaknuvan kartumarer vighātaṃ svakarmarakṣāṃ ca paraṃ ṣrayeta
Bhk ekena saṃdhiḥ
kalaho 'pareṇa kāryo 'bhito vā prasamīkṣya vṛddhim
Bhk evaṃ prayuñjīta jigīṣuretā nītīr vijānannahitā''tmasāram
Bhk tvayā tu loke janito virāgaḥ
prakopitaṃ maṇḍalamindramukhyam
Bhk rāme tu rājan
viparītametat paśyāmi
tenā 'bhyadhikaṃ vipakṣam
Bhk ekena vālī nihataḥ śareṇa suhṛttamas te
racitaś ca rājā
Bhk yadaiva sugrīvakapiḥ pareṇa
tadaiva kāryaṃ bhavato vinaṣṭam
Bhk prākāramātrā''varaṇaḥ prabhāvaḥ kharā''dibhir yo nihatais tavā'bhūt
Bhk laṅkāpradāhā'kṣavadhadrubhaṅgaiḥ klāmyatyasāvapyadhunā 'timātram
Bhk ṣaḍvargavaśyaḥ parimūḍhabandhu rucchinnamitro viguṇairupetaḥ
Bhk mā pādayuddhaṃ dviradena kārṣīr nama kṣitīndraṃ praṇatopabhogyam
Bhk rāmo 'pi dārā''haraṇena tapto
vayaṃ hatair bandhubhirātmatulyaiḥ
Bhk taptasya taptena yathā ''yaso naḥ saṃdhiḥ pareṇā 'stu
vimuñca sītām
Bhk saṃdhukṣitaṃ maṇḍalacaṇḍavātai ramarṣatīkṣṇaṃ kṣitipālatejaḥ
Bhk sāmā'mbhasā śāntimupaitu rājan 
prasīda jīvāma sabandhubhṛtyāḥ
Bhk apakvakumbhāviva bhaṅgabhājau rājanniyātāṃ maraṇaṃ samānau
Bhk vīrye sthitaḥ kiṃtu kṛtā'nurāgo rāmo bhavaṃś cottamabhūrivairī
Bhk daṇḍena kośena ca manyase cet prakṛṣṭamātmānamares tathāpi
Bhk riktasya pūrṇena vṛthā vināśaḥ pūrṇasya bhaṅge bahu hīyate tu
Bhk kliṣṭā''tmabhṛtyaḥ parimṛgyasampan mānī yatetā 'pi sasaṃśaye 'rthe
Bhk saṃdehamārohati yaḥ kṛtā'rtho
nūnaṃ ratiṃ tasya karoti na śrīḥ
Bhk śakyānyadoṣāṇi mahāphalāni samārabhetopanayan samāptim
Bhk karmāṇi rājā vihitā'nurāgo
viparyaye syād vitathaḥ prayāsaḥ
Bhk jetuṃ na śakyo nṛpatiḥ sunītir doṣaḥ kṣayā''diḥ kalahe dhruvaś ca
Bhk phalaṃ na kiṃcin na śubhā samāptiḥ
kṛtā'nurāgaṃ bhūvi saṃtyajā 'rim
Bhk tvanmitranāśo
nijamitralābhaḥ
sametasainyaḥ sa ca mitrakṛcchre
Bhk bhogyo vaśaḥ paśya śareṇa śatroḥ prasādhito vālivadhe na ko 'rthaḥ
Bhk lobhād bhayād vā 'bhigataḥ kapīndro na rāghavaṃ
yena bhaved vibhedyaḥ
Bhk sthitaḥ satāṃ vartmani labdharājyaḥ pratipriyaṃ so 'bhyagamac cikīrṣuḥ
Bhk phalāśino nirjharakuñjabhājo divyā'ṅganā'naṅgarasā'nabhijñāḥ
Bhk nyagjātayo ratnavarairalabhyā mukhyāḥ kapīnāmapi nopajapyāḥ
Bhk kṛtā'bhiṣeko yuvarājarājye sugrīvarājena sutā'viśeṣam
Bhk tārāvidheyena kathaṃ vikāraṃ tārāsuto yāsyati rākṣasā'rtham
Bhk paśyāmi rāmādadhikaṃ samaṃ vā nā 'nyaṃ
virodhe yamupāśrayema
Bhk dattvā varaṃ sā'nuśayaḥ svayambhū rindrā''dayaḥ pūrvataraṃ viruddhāḥ
Bhk durgā''śritānāṃ bahunā 'pi rājan 
kālena pārṣṇigrahaṇā''dihetuḥ
Bhk durgoparodhaṃ na ca kurvato 'sti śatroś cireṇā 'pi daśā''sya  hāniḥ
Bhk śastraṃ tarūrvīdharamambu pānaṃ vṛttiḥ phalair
no gajavājināryaḥ
Bhk rāṣṭraṃ na paścān
na jano'bhirakṣyaḥ
kiṃ duḥsthamācakṣva bhavet pareṣām
Bhk saṃdhānamevā 'stu pareṇa tasmān
nā'nyo 'bhyupāyo 'sti nirūpyamāṇaḥ
Bhk nūnaṃ visaṃdhau tvayi sarvametan neṣyanti nāśaṃ kapayo 'cireṇa
Bhk vibhīṣaṇoktaṃ bahu manyamānaḥ pronnamya dehaṃ pariṇāmanamram
Bhk skhaladvalir vārdhakakampramūrdhā mātāmaho rāvaṇamityuvāca
Bhk ekaḥ padātiḥ puruṣo dhanuṣmān yo 'nekamāyāni viyadgatāni
Bhk rakṣaḥsahasrāṇi caturdaśā ''rdīt
kā tatra vo mānuṣamātraśaṅkā
Bhk brahmarṣibhir nūnamayaṃ sadevaiḥ saṃtāpitau rātricarakṣayāya
Bhk narā''kṛtir vānarasainyaśālī jagatyajayyo vihito 'bhyupāyaḥ
Bhk vajrā'bhighātairavirugṇamūrteḥ pheṇair jalānāmasurasya mūrdhnaḥ
Bhk cakāra bhedaṃ mṛdubhir mahendro yathā
tathaitat kimapīti bodhyam
Bhk kva strīviṣahyāḥ karajāḥ
kva vakṣo daityasya śailendraśilāviśālam
Bhk saṃpaśyataitad dyusadāṃ sunītaṃ
bibheda tais tan narasiṃhamūrtiḥ
Bhk pramādavāṃs tvaṃ kṣatadharmavartmā gato munīnāmapi śatrubhāvam
Bhk kulasya śāntiṃ bahu manyase cet kuruṣva rājendra 
vibhīṣaṇoktam
Bhk ghoṣeṇa tena pratilabdhasaṃjño nidrā''vilā'kṣaḥ ṣrutakāryasāraḥ
Bhk sphuradghanaḥ sā'mburivā 'ntarīkṣe vākyaṃ tato 'bhāṣata kumbhakarṇaḥ
Bhk kriyāsamārambhagato 'bhyupāyo
nṛdravyasampat sahadeśakalā
Bhk vipatpratīkārayutā 'rthasiddhir mantrā'ṅgametāni vadanti pañca
Bhk na niścitā'rthaṃ samayaṃ ca deśaṃ kriyā'bhyupāyā''diṣu yo 'tiyāyāt
Bhk sa prāpnuyān mantraphalaṃ na mānī kāle vipanne kṣaṇadācarendra 
Bhk auṣṇyaṃ tyajen madhyagato 'pi bhānuḥ
śaityaṃ niśāyāmathavā himāṃśuḥ
Bhk anarthamūlaṃ bhuvanā'vamānī manye na mānaṃ piśitāśinātha 
Bhk tathā 'pi vaktuṃ prasabhaṃ yatante yan madvidhāḥ siddhimabhīpsavas tvām
Bhk vilomaceṣṭaṃ vihitā'vahāsāḥ parair hi tat snehamayais tamobhiḥ
Bhk krūrāḥ kriyāḥ
grāmyasukheṣu saṅgaḥ
puṇyasya yaḥ saṃkṣayaheturuktaḥ
Bhk niṣevito 'sau bhavatā 'timātraṃ phalatyavalgu dhruvameva rājan 
Bhk dattaṃ na kiṃ
ke viṣayā na bhuktāḥ
sthito 'smi vā kaṃ paribhūya noccaiḥ
Bhk itthaṃ kṛtā'rthasya mama dhruvaṃ syān mutyus tvadarthe yadi
kiṃ na labdham
Bhk kiṃ durnayais tvayyuditair mṛṣā'rthair vīryeṇa vaktā 'smi raṇe samādhim
Bhk tasmin prasupte punaritthamuktvā vibhīṣaṇo 'bhāṣata rākṣasendram
Bhk nimittaśūnyaiḥ sthagitā rajobhir diśo
marudbhir vikṛtair vilolaiḥ
Bhk svabhāvahīnair mṛgapakṣighoṣaiḥ krandanti bhartāramivā 'bhipannam
Bhk utpātajaṃ chidramasau vivasvān vyādāya vaktrā''kṛti lokabhīṣmam
Bhk attuṃ janān dhūsararaśmirāśiḥ siṃho yathā kīrṇasaṭo 'bhyudeti
Bhk mārgaṃ gato gotragurur bhṛgūṇā magastinā 'dhyāsitavindhyaśṛṅgam
Bhk saṃdṛśyate śakrapurohito 'hni
kṣmāṃ kampayantyo nipatanti colkāḥ
Bhk māṃsaṃ hatānāmiva rākṣasānā māśaṃsavaḥ krūragiro ruvantaḥ
Bhk kravyā'śino dīptakṛśānuvaktrā bhrāmyantyabhītāḥ paritaḥ puraṃ naḥ
Bhk payo ghaṭodhnīrapi gā duhanti mandaṃ vivarṇaṃ virasaṃ ca gopāḥ
Bhk havyeṣu kīṭopajanaḥ sakeśo na dīpyate 'gniḥ susamindhano 'pi
Bhk tasmāt kuru tvaṃ pratikāramasmin snehān mayā rāvaṇa 
bhāṣyamāṇaḥ
Bhk vadanti duḥkhaṃ hyanujīvivṛtte sthitāḥ padasthaṃ pariṇāmapathyam
Bhk virugṇasaṃkīrṇavipannabhinnaiḥ pakṣuṇṇasaṃhrīṇaśitā'stravṛkṇaiḥ
Bhk yāvan narā'śair na ripuḥ śava'śān saṃtarpayatyānama tāvadasmai
Bhk bhrūbhaṅgamādhāya vihāya dhairyaṃ vibhīṣaṇaṃ bhīṣaṇarūkṣacakṣuḥ
Bhk giraṃ jagādograpadāmudagraḥ svaṃ sphāvayan śakraripuḥ prabhāvam
Bhk śilā tariṣyatyudake na parṇaṃ
dhvāntaṃ raveḥ syantsyati
vahnirindoḥ
Bhk jetā paro 'haṃ yudhi jeṣyamāṇas tulyāni manyasva pulastyanaptaḥ 
Bhk anirvṛtaṃ bhūtiṣu gūḍhavairaṃ satkārakāle 'pi kṛtā 'bhyasūyam
Bhk vibhinnakarmā''śayavāk kule no mā jñāticelaṃ
bhuvi kasyacid bhūt
Bhk icchantyabhīkṣṇaṃ kṣayamātmano 'pi na jñātayas tulyakulasya lakṣmīm
Bhk namanti śatrūn

Bhk tūrṇamanvasṛpad rāma mānanandac ca vānarān
Bhk atatvarac ca tān yoddhumaciceṣṭac ca rāghavau
Bhk kumbhakarṇo nyavartiṣṭa
raṇe'yutsanta vānarāḥ
Bhk aviveṣṭan nṛpā''deśādārukṣaṃś cā''śu rākṣasam
Bhk tānadhāvīt samārūḍhāṃs te 'pyusraṃsiṣatā ''kulāḥ
Bhk agrasiṣṭa
vyadhāviṣṭa
samāślikṣac ca nirdayam
Bhk te cā 'pyaghoriṣur ghoraṃ
raktaṃ cā 'vamiṣur mukhaiḥ
Bhk sa cā'pi rudhirair mattaḥ sveṣāmapyadayiṣṭa na
Bhk agrahīc cā ''yuranyeṣāmaruddha ca parākramam
Bhk saṃtrastānāṃapāhāri sattvaṃ ca vanavāsinām
Bhk acchedi lakṣmaṇenā'sya kirīṭaṃ kavacaṃ tathā
Bhk abhedi ca śarair dehaḥ prāśaṃsīt taṃ niśācaraḥ
Bhk aspardhiṣṭa ca rāmeṇa tenā 'syā 'kṣipsateṣavaḥ
Bhk yairaghāni kharo
vālī
mārīco
dūṣaṇas tathā
Bhk avāmaṃsta sa tān darpāt
prodayaṃsīc ca mudgaram
Bhk vāyavyā'streṇa taṃ pāṇiṃ rāmo 'cchaitsīt sahā''yudham
Bhk ādīpi taruhasto 'sā vadhāvīc cā 'risaṃmukham
Bhk savṛkṣamacchidat tasya śakrā'streṇa karaṃ nṛpaḥ
Bhk jaṅghe cā 'śīśatad bāṇairaprāsīdiṣubhir mukham
Bhk aindreṇa hṛdaye 'vyātsīt
so 'dhyavātsīc ca gāṃ hataḥ
Bhk apikṣātāṃ sahasre dve taddehena vanaukasām
Bhk astāviṣuḥ surā rāmaṃ
diśaḥ prāpan niśācarāḥ

Bhk arodīd rāvaṇo 'śocīn
mohaṃ cā 'śiśriyat param
Bhk apaprathad guṇān bhrāturacikīrtac ca vikramam
Bhk kruddhena kumbhakarṇena ye 'dirṣiśata śatravaḥ
Bhk kathaṃ nvajīviṣus te ca
sa cā 'mṛta mahābalaḥ
Bhk ayuyutsiṣatā ''śvāsya kumārā rāvaṇaṃ tataḥ
Bhk devāntako 'tikāyaś ca triśirāḥ sa narāntakaḥ
Bhk te cāṃ''hiṣata saṃgrāmaṃ balino rāvaṇā''tmajāḥ
Bhk yuddhonmattaṃ ca mattaṃ ca rājā rakṣārthamāñjihat
Bhk sutānāṃ niragātāṃ tau rākṣasau raṇapaṇḍitau
Bhk tairajeṣata sainyāni
dviṣo 'kāriṣatā ''kulāḥ
Bhk parvatāniva te bhūmāvacaiṣur vānarottamān
Bhk aṅgadena samaṃ yoddhumaghaṭiṣṭa narāntakaḥ
Bhk praiṣiṣad rākṣasaḥ prāsaṃ
so 'sphoṭīdaṅgadorasi
Bhk aśvān vālisuto 'hiṃsīdatatāḍac ca muṣṭinā
Bhk rāvaṇiś cā 'vyatho yoddhumārabdha ca mahīṃ gataḥ
Bhk tasyā 'hāriṣata prāṇā muṣṭinā vālisūnunā
Bhk prādudruvaṃs tataḥ kruddhāḥ sarve rāvaṇayo'ṅgadam
Bhk tato nīlahanūmantau rāvaṇīnavaveṣṭatām
Bhk akāriṣṭāṃ girīṃs tuṅgānarautsīt triśirāḥ śaraiḥ
Bhk parigheṇā 'vadhiṣṭā 'tha raṇe devāntako balī
Bhk muṣṭinā 'dadarat tasya mūrdhānaṃ mārutā''tmajaḥ
Bhk adīdipat tato vīryaṃ
nīlaṃ cā'pīpiḍac charaiḥ
Bhk yuddhonmattas
tu nīlena giriṇā'nāyi saṃkṣayam
Bhk ababhrājat tataḥ śaktiṃ triśirāḥ pavanā''tmaje
Bhk hanūmatā kṣatās tasya raṇe 'mṛṣata vājinaḥ
Bhk asrasac cā''hato mūrdhni
khaḍgaṃ cā 'jīharad dviṣā
Bhk prāṇānaujjhīc ca khaḍgena chinnais tenaiva mūrdhabhiḥ

Bhk sahasrahariṇā 'krīḍīdatikāyas tato raṇe
Bhk rathenā 'vivyathac cā'rīn
vyacārīc ca niraṅkuśaḥ
Bhk vibhīṣaṇena so 'khyāyi rāghavasya mahārathaḥ
Bhk atastambhadayaṃ vajraṃ
svayambhuvamatūtuṣat

raṇe 'rakṣīc ca rākṣasān

yamasyā 'hnoṣṭa vikramam
Bhk devā''haveṣvadīpiṣṭa
nā 'janiṣṭā 'sya sādhvasam
Bhk eṣa rāvaṇirāpādi vānarāṇāṃ bhayaṅkaraḥ
Bhk āhvatā 'tha sa kākutsthaṃ dhanuś cā 'pusphurad guru
Bhk saumitriḥ sarpavat siṃhamārdidat taṃ mahā''have
Bhk tau prāvīvṛtatāṃ jetuṃ śarajālānyanekaśaḥ
Bhk acchaittāṃ ca mahā''tmānau
ciramaśramatāṃ na ca
Bhk tathā tāvāsthatāṃ bāṇānatāniṣṭāṃ tamo yathā
Bhk sauryā''gneye vyakāriṣṭāmastre rākṣasalakṣmaṇau
Bhk te copāgamatā nāśaṃ samāsādya parasparam
Bhk abibhrajat tataḥ śastramaiṣīkaṃ rākṣaso raṇe
Bhk tadapyadhvasadāsādya māhendraṃ lakṣmaṇeritam
Bhk tataḥ saumitrirasmārṣīdadeviṣṭa ca durjayam
Bhk brahmā'straṃ
tena mūrdhānamadadhvaṃsan naradviṣaḥ
Bhk tato 'krandīd daśagrīvas tamāśiśvasadindrajit
Bhk nirayāsīc ca saṃkruddhaḥ
prārcicac ca svayambhuvam
Bhk ahauṣīt kṛṣṇavartmānaṃ
samayaṣṭā 'stramaṇḍalam
Bhk so 'labdha brahmaṇaḥ śastraṃ syandanaṃ ca jayā''vaham
Bhk tamadhyāsiṣṭa dīprā'gramamodiṣṭa ca rāvaṇiḥ
Bhk channarūpas tato 'kartīd dehān rāvaṇavidviṣām
Bhk saptaṣaṣṭiṃ plavaṅgānāṃ koṭīr bāṇairasūṣupat
Bhk niśā'nte rāvaṇiḥ kruddho rāghavau ca vyamūmuhat
Bhk apisphavat svasāmarthyamagūhīt sāyakair diśaḥ
Bhk aghorīc ca mahāghoraṃ
gatvā
praiṣīc ca rāvaṇam
Bhk vibhīṣaṇas tato 'bodhi sasphurau rāmalakṣmaṇau
Bhk apārīt sa gṛhītolko hataśeṣān plavaṅgamān
Bhk mā śociṣṭa
raghuvyāghrau nā'mṛṣātāmiti bruvan

Bhk tatraiṣaj jāmbavān prāṇīdudamīlīc ca locane
Bhk paulastyaṃ cā'gadīt kaccidajīvīn mārutā''tmajaḥ
Bhk tasya kṣeme mahārāja 
nā 'mṛṣmahyakhilā vayam
Bhk paulastyo 'śiśravat taṃ ca jīvantaṃ pavanā''tmajam
Bhk āyiṣṭa mārutis tatra
tau cā 'pyahṛṣatāṃ tataḥ

sa ca prāpi mahāgiriḥ

Bhk niracāyi yadā bhedo nauṣadhīnāṃ hanūmatā
Bhk sarva eva samāhāri tadā śailaḥ mahauṣadhiḥ
Bhk prāṇiṣur nihatāḥ kecit

vyajṛmbhiṣata cā'pare

vīryaṃ cā'dhiṣatā'dhikam

prāpatāṃ tau plavaṅgamān

prapalāyiṣṭa cā''kulam

Bhk ahārṣīc ca śiraḥ kṣipraṃ yūpākṣasya nirākulaḥ
Bhk śarīraṃ lohitākṣasya nyabhāṅkṣīd dvividas tadā

Bhk grīvāṃ cā 'sya tathākrākṣīdajijīvad yathā na tam
Bhk samagatakapisainyaṃ sammadenā 'timātraṃ

yad vinayā''gatam

sītāṃ rāghavaḥ kāmayiṣyate

 ityetat prahastena ca bhāṣitam

Bhk bhallairavidhyannugrā'grairatṛṃhaṃs tomarairalam
Bhk āsyan plavaṅgamā vṛkṣānadhunvan bhūdharair bhṛśam
Bhk ahiṃsan muṣṭibhiḥ kroghādadaśan daśanairapi
Bhk prādunvan jānubhis tūrṇamatudaṃs talakūrparaiḥ
Bhk prāhiṇvannarimuktāni śastrāṇi vividhāni ca
Bhk atṛṇeṭ śakrajic chatrūnabhrāmyac ca samantataḥ
Bhk adhvanac ca mahāghoraṃ
na ca kaṃcana nā'dunot
Bhk nā'jānan sandadhānaṃ taṃ
dhanur naikṣanta bibhratam
Bhk neṣūnacetannasyantaṃ
hatās tenā 'vidur dviṣaḥ
Bhk aśṛṇvannanyataḥ śabdaṃ
prapalāyanta cā 'nyataḥ
Bhk ākrandamanyato'kurvaṃs tenā 'hanyanta cā'nyataḥ
Bhk prāloṭhanta
vyabhidyanta
parito raktamasravan
Bhk paryaśrāmyannatṛpyaṃś ca kṣatās tenā 'mriyanta ca
Bhk saumitrirākulas tasmin brahmā'straṃ sarvarakṣasām
Bhk nidhanāyā ''juhūṣat taṃ vyṣṭabhnād raghunandanaḥ
Bhk tato māyāmayīṃ sītāṃ ghnan khaḍgena viyadgataḥ
Bhk adṛśyatendrajid
vākyamavadat taṃ marutsutaḥ
Bhk mā 'parādhnodiyaṃ kiṃcidabhraśyat patyurantikāt
Bhk sītāṃ rākṣasa 
mā smaināṃ nigṛhṇāḥ pāpa  duḥkhitām
Bhk pīḍākaramamitrāṇāṃ kartavyamiti śakrajit
Bhk abravīt khaḍgakṛṣṭaś ca tasyā mūrdhānamacchinat
Bhk yatkṛte 'rīn vyagṛhṇīma
samudramatarāma ca
Bhk sā hateti vadan rāmamupātiṣṭhan marutsutaḥ
Bhk tataḥ prāmuhyatāṃ vīrau rāghavāvarutāṃ tathā
Bhk uṣṇaṃ ca prāṇatāṃ dīrghamuccair vyākrośatāṃ tathā
Bhk tāvabhāṣata paulastyo mā sma praruditaṃ yuvām
Bhk dhruvaṃ sa mohayitvā'smān pāpo'gacchannikumbhilām
Bhk mā sma tiṣṭhata
tatrastho vadhyo 'smāvahutā'nalaḥ
Bhk astre brahmaśirasyugre syandane cā 'nupārjite
Bhk brahmā 'dadhād vadhaṃ tasya tasmin karmaṇyasaṃsthite
Bhk prāyacchadājñāṃ saumitrer yuthapānāṃ ca rāghavaḥ
Bhk tāṃ pratyaicchan susaṃpritās tatas te savibhīṣaṇāḥ
Bhk nikumbhilāṃ samabhyāyan
nyarudhyanta ca rākṣasaiḥ
Bhk dikpālaiḥ kadanaṃ tatra sene prākurutāṃ mahat
Bhk aitāṃ rakṣāṃsi nirjitya drutaṃ paulastyalakṣmaṇau
Bhk tatrendrajitamaikṣetāṃ kṛtadhiṣṇyaṃ samāhitam
Bhk so 'juhot kṛṣṇavartmānamāmanan mantramuttamam
Bhk adhyāyac chakrajid brahma
samādheracalan na ca
Bhk tamāhvayata saumitriragarjac ca bhayaṃkaram
Bhk akupyadindrajit tatra
pitṛvyaṃ cā'gadad vacaḥ
Bhk tvamatrā 'jāyathā
deha ihā 'puṣyat surā'miṣaiḥ
Bhk ihā 'jīva ihaiva tvaṃ krūramārabhathāḥ katham
Bhk nā'paśyaḥ pāṇimārdraṃ tvaṃ
bandhutvaṃ nā'pyapaikṣathāḥ
Bhk adharmān nā 'trasaḥ pāpa 
lokavādān na cā 'bibheḥ
Bhk dharmaduṣaṇa 
nūnaṃ tvaṃ nā 'jānā
nā 'śṛṇoridam
Bhk nirākṛtya yathā bandhūn laghutvaṃ yātyasaṃśayam
Bhk pitṛvyeṇa tato vākyamabhyadhīyata śakrajit
Bhk mithyā mā sma vyatikrāmo
macchīlaṃ mā na badhyathāh
Bhk satyaṃ samabhavaṃ vaṃśe pāpānāṃ rakṣasāmaham
Bhk na tvajāyata me śīlaṃ tādṛk
yādṛk pitus tava
Bhk kṣayā''vaheṣu doṣeṣu vāryamāṇo mayā 'ramat
Bhk daśagrīvaṃ 'hametasmādatyajaṃ
na tu vidviṣan
Bhk parasvānyārjayan
nārīranyadīyāḥ parāmṛśat
Bhk vyajighṛkṣat surān nityaṃ
prāmādyad guṇināṃ hite
Bhk āśaṅkata suhṛdbandhūnavṛddhān bahvamanyata
Bhk doṣairaramataibhis te pitā 'tyajyata yair mayā
Bhk tatoruṣyadanardac ca
dviviṃśatibhireva ca
Bhk śarairatāḍayad bandhuṃ
pañcaviṃśatibhir nṛpam
Bhk rāvaṇis tasya saumitriramathnāc caturo hayān
Bhk sāgarathiṃ cā 'lunād bāṇairabhanak syandanaṃ tathā
Bhk saumitrimakirad bāṇaiḥ parito rāvaṇis tataḥ
Bhk tāvasphāvayatāṃ śāktiṃ
bāṇāṃś cā'kiratāṃ muhuḥ
Bhk vāruṇaṃ lakṣmaṇo'kṣipyadakṣipad raudramindrajit
Bhk te parasparamāsādya śastre nāśamagacchatām
Bhk āsuraṃ rākṣasaḥ śastraṃ tato ghoraṃ vyasarjayat
Bhk tasmān nirapatad bhūri śilāśūleṣṭimudgaram
Bhk māheśvareṇa saumitrirastabhnāt tat sudurjayam
Bhk tato raudrasamāyuktaṃ māhendraṃ lakṣmaṇo'smarat
Bhk tenā''gamyata ghoreṇa
śiraś cā 'hriyata dviṣaḥ
Bhk atuṣyannamarāḥ sarve
prāhṛṣyan kapiyūthapāḥ
Bhk paryaṣvajata saumitriṃ
mūrdhnyajighrac ca rāghavaḥ
Bhk arodīd rākṣasā'nīkamarodan nṛbhujāṃ patiḥ
Bhk maithilyai cā 'śapaddhantuṃ tāṃ prākramata cā''turaḥ
Bhk ayuktamidam tyanye tamāptāḥ pratyavārayan
Bhk nyarundhaṃś cā 'sya panthānaṃ bandhutā śucamāruṇat
Bhk āsphāyatā 'sya vīratvamamarṣaś cā 'pyatāyata
Bhk rāvaṇasya tataḥ sainyaṃ samastamayuyutsayat
Bhk agnīnavarivasyaṃś ca te
'namasyaṃś ca śaṅkaram
Bhk dvijānaprīṇayan śāntyai yātudhānā bhavadbhiyaḥ
Bhk paritaḥ paryavād vāyurājyagandhir manoramaḥ
Bhk aśrūyata sa puṇyāhaḥ svastighoṣaḥ samuccaran
Bhk yoddhāro 'bibharuḥ śāntyai sā'kṣataṃ vāri mūrdhabhiḥ
Bhk ratnāni cā 'dadur gāś ca
samavāñchannathā''śiṣaḥ
Bhk adihaṃś candanaiḥ śubhrair
vicitraṃ samavastrayan
Bhk adhārayan srajaḥ kāntā
varma cā 'nye 'dadhur drutam
Bhk samakṣṇuvata śastrāṇi
prāmṛjan khaḍgasaṃhatīḥ
Bhk gajā''dīni samārohan
prātiṣṭhantā ''tha satvarāḥ
Bhk apūrayan nabhaḥ śabdo balasaṃvartasaṃbhavaḥ
Bhk apūryanta ca digbhāgās tumulais tūryanisvanaiḥ
Bhk āsīd dvāreṣu saṃghaṭṭo rathā'śvadviparakṣasām
Bhk samahānanimittaiś ca samabhūyata bhīṣaṇaiḥ
Bhk kapayo 'bibhayus tasminnabhañjaṃś ca mahādrumān
Bhk prodakhāyan girīṃs tūrṇamagṛhṇaṃś ca mahāśilāḥ
Bhk tataḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ prāharan kapirākṣasāḥ
Bhk anyonyenā 'bhyabhūyanta
vimardamasahanta ca
Bhk prāvardhata rajo bhaumaṃ
tad vyāśnuta diśo daśa
Bhk parā''tmīyavivekaṃ ca prāmuṣṇāt kapirakṣasām
Bhk tato 'dviṣur nirāloke svebhyo 'nyebhyaś ca rākṣasāḥ
Bhk adviṣan vānarāś caiva vānarebhyo 'pi nirdayāḥ
Bhk aghuraṃs te mahāghoramaścyotannatha śoṇitam
Bhk samapadyata raktena samantāt tena kardamaḥ
Bhk gambhīrāḥ prāvahan nadyaḥ
samajāyanta ca hradāḥ
Bhk vṛddhaṃ ca tad rajo 'śāmyat
samavedyanta ca dviṣaḥ
Bhk tato 'citrīyatā 'straughair dhanuś cā 'dhūnayan mahat
Bhk rāmaḥ samīhitaṃ tasya nā'cetan sve na cā 'pare
Bhk chinnānaikṣanta bhinnāṃś ca samantād rāmasāyukaiḥ
Bhk kruṣṭaṃ hāheti cā 'śṛṇvan na ca rāmaṃ nyarūpayan
Bhk abhinac chatrusaṃghātānakṣuṇad vājikuñjaram
Bhk apinaṭ ca rathā'nīkaṃ
na cā 'jñāyata saṃcaran
Bhk daśa dantisahasrāṇi rathināṃ ca mahā''tmanām
Bhk caturdaśa sahasrāṇi sā''rohāṇāṃ ca vājinām
Bhk lakṣe ca dve padātīnāṃ rāghaveṇa dhanurbhṛtā
Bhk anīyantāṣṭame bhāge divasasya parikṣayam
Bhk yamalokamivā'grathnād
rudrā''krīḍamivā 'karot
Bhk śailairivā 'cinod bhūmiṃ bṛhadbhī rākṣasair hataiḥ
Bhk astuvan devagandharvā
vyasmayanta plavaṅgamāḥ
Bhk kapīndre'tanyata prītiḥ
paulastyo'manyatā'dbhutam
Bhk rākṣasyaḥ prārudannuccaiḥ
prājugupsanta rāvaṇam
Bhk amuhyad bālavṛddhaṃ ca
samarauditaro janaḥ
Bhk sarvataś cā'bhayaṃ prāpnon naicchan nṛbhyas tu rāvaṇaḥ
Bhk phalaṃ tasyedamabhyāyād duruktasyeti cā 'bruvan
Bhk tato 'dhāvan mahāghoraṃ rathamāsthāya rāvaṇaḥ
Bhk akṣmāyata mahī
gṛdhrāḥ samārāryanta bhīṣaṇāḥ
Bhk meghāḥ savidyuto 'varṣaṃś celaknopaṃ ca śoṇitam
Bhk avān bhīmā nabhasvantaḥ
prāruvannaśivāḥ śivāḥ
Bhk āṭāṭyatā 'vamatyā 'sau durnimittāni saṃyuge
Bhk adhunod dhanurastraughaiḥ praurṇonūyata vidviṣaḥ
Bhk vyanāśayaṃs tataḥ śatrūn sugrīvā'stā mahībhṛtaḥ
Bhk tato vyarasadaglāyadadhyśeta mahītalam
Bhk āścyotad rudhiraṃ
toyamalasac cā'ti vihvalam
Bhk aśīyata nṛmāṃsā'dāṃ balaṃ sugrīvabādhitam
Bhk virūpākṣas tato krīḍat saṃgrāme mattahastinā
Bhk muṣṭinā'dālayat tasya mūrdhānaṃ vānarā'dhipaḥ
Bhk acūrṇayac ca yūpākṣaṃ śilayā tadanantaram
Bhk saṃkruddho muṣṭinā'tubhnādaṅgado'laṃ mahodaram
Bhk tato 'kuṣṇād daśagrīvaḥ kruddhaḥ prāṇān vanaukasām
Bhk agopāyac ca rakṣāṃsi diśaś cā 'rīnabhājayat
Bhk ālokayat sa kākutsthamadhṛṣṇod
ghoramadhvanat
Bhk dhanurabhramayad bhīmamabhīṣayata vidviṣaḥ
Bhk āskandal lakṣmaṇaṃ bānairatyakrāmac ca taṃ drutam
Bhk rāmamabhyadravaj jiṣṇuraskunāc ceṣuvṛṣṭibhiḥ
Bhk apauhad bāṇavarṣaṃ tad bhallai rāmo nirākulaḥ
Bhk pratyaskunod daṣagrīvaṃ śarairāśīviṣopamaiḥ
Bhk maṇḍalānyāṭatāṃ citramacchittāṃ śastrasaṃhatīḥ
Bhk jagad vismāpayetāṃ tau
na ca vīrāvasīdatām
Bhk vyoma prācinutāṃ bāṇaiḥ
kṣmāmakṣmāpayatāṃ gataiḥ
Bhk abhittāṃ tūrṇamanyonyaṃ śikṣāś cā 'tanutāṃ muhuḥ
Bhk samādhattā ''suraṃ śastraṃ rākṣasaḥ krūravikramaḥ
Bhk tadakṣaran mahāsarpān vyāghrasiṃhāṃś ca bhīṣaṇān
Bhk nyaṣedhat pāvakā'streṇa rāmas tad rākṣasas tataḥ
Bhk adīvyad raudramatyugraṃ
musalā''dyagalat tataḥ
Bhk gāndharveṇa nyavidyat tat kṣitīndro
'tha narā'śanaḥ
Bhk sarvamarmasu kākutstha maumbhat tīkṣṇaiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ
Bhk tatas triśirasaṃ tasya prāvṛścal lakṣmaṇo dhvajam
Bhk amathnāt sārathiṃ cā''śu
bhūribhiś cā 'tudaccharaiḥ
Bhk aśvān vibhīṣano 'tubhnāt syandanaṃ cā'kṣiṇod drutam
Bhk nā'kṣubhnād rākṣaso
bhrātuḥ śaktiṃ codavṛhad gurum
Bhk tāmāpatantīṃ saumitris tridhā'kṛntacchilīmukhaiḥ
Bhk aśabdāyanta paśyantas tataḥ kruddho niśācaraḥ
Bhk aṣṭaghaṇṭāṃ mahāśaktimudayacchan mahattarām
Bhk rāmā'nujaṃ tayā 'vidhyat
sa mahīṃ vyasurāśrayat
Bhk rāghavasyā'bhṛśāyanta sāyakās
tairupadrutaḥ
Bhk tatas tūrṇaṃ daśagrīvo raṇakṣmā paryaśeṣayat
Bhk sasphurasyodakarṣac ca saumitreḥ śaktimagrajaḥ
Bhk asiñcadoṣadhīs tā yāḥ samānītā hanūmatā
Bhk udajīvat sumitrābhūr bhrātā ''śliṣyata tamāyatam
Bhk sanyaṅ mūrdhanyupāśiṅgha dapṛcchac ca nirāmayam
Bhk tataḥ prodasahan sarve yoddhumabhyadravat parān
Bhk akṛcchrāyata ca prāpto rathenā 'nyena 'rāvaṇaḥ
Bhk bhūmiṣṭhasyā 'samaṃ yuddhaṃ rathastheneti mātaliḥ
Bhk āharad rathamatyugraṃ saśastraṃ maghavā ''jñayā
Bhk so 'dhyaṣṭhīyata rāmeṇa
śastraṃ pāśupataṃ tataḥ
Bhk nirāsyata daśā''syas
tacchakrā'streṇājayan nṛpaḥ
Bhk tataḥ śatamahasreṇa rāmaḥ praurṇon niśācaram
Bhk bāṇānāmakṣiṇod dhuryān
sārathiṃ cā'dunod drutam
Bhk adṛśyantā 'nimittāni
prāhvalat kṣitimaṇḍalam
Bhk rāvaṇaḥ prāhiṇocchūlaṃ
śaktiṃ caindīṃ mahīpatiḥ
Bhk tābhyāmanyonyamāsādya samavāpyata saṃśamaḥ
Bhk lakṣeṇa patriṇāṃ vakṣaḥ kruddho rāmasya rākṣasaḥ
Bhk astṛṇādadhikaṃ rāmas tato 'devata sāyakaiḥ
Bhk aklāmyadrāvaṇas
tasya sūto rathamanāśayat
Bhk rākṣaso'tarjayat sūtaṃ punaś cā'ḍhaukayad ratham
Bhk nirāsyetāmubhaubāṇānubhau dhuryānavidhyatām
Bhk ubhāvakṛntatāṃ ketūnāvyathetāmubhau na tau
Bhk adīpyetāmubhau dhṛṣṇū
prāyuñjātāṃ ca naipuṇam
Bhk ubhau māyāṃ vyatāyetāṃ
vīrau nā 'śrāmyatāmubhau
Bhk maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi kṣipramākrāmatāmubhau
Bhk na cobhāvapyalakṣyetāṃ
yantārāvāhatāmubhau
Bhk syandanau samapṛcyetāmubhayor dīptavājinau
Bhk tato māyāmayān mūrdhno rākṣaso 'prathayadraṇe
Bhk rāmeṇaikaśataṃ teṣāṃ prāvṛścyata śilīmukhaiḥ
Bhk samakṣubhnannudanvantaḥ
prākampanta mahībhṛtaḥ
Bhk santrāsamabibhaḥ śakruḥ
praiṃkhacca
kṣubhitā kṣitiḥ
Bhk tato mātalinā śastramasmaryata mahīpateḥ
Bhk vadhāya rāvaṇasyograṃ svayambhūr yadakalpayat
Bhk nabhasvān yasya vājeṣu
phale tigmāṃśupāvakau
Bhk gurutvaṃ merusaṅkāśaṃ
dehaḥ sūkṣmo viyanmayaḥ
Bhk rājitaṃ gāruḍaiḥ pakṣair viśveṣāṃ ghāma tejasām
Bhk smṛtaṃ tad rāvaṇaṃ bhittvā sughoraṃ bhuvyaśāyayat
Bhk ābadhnan kapivadanāni saṃprasādaṃ
prāśaṃsat surasamitir nṛpaṃ jitā 'rim
Bhk anyeṣāṃ vigatapariplavā digantāḥ
paulastyo'juṣata śucaṃ vipannabandhuḥ
Bhk vyaśnute sma tataḥ śoko nābhisambandhasambhavaḥ
Bhk vibhīṣaṇamasāvuccai roditi sma daśā''nanam
Bhk bhūmau śete daśagrīvo mahārhaśayanocitaḥ
Bhk nekṣate vihvalaṃ māṃ ca
na me vācaṃ prayacchati
Bhk vipāko'yaṃ daśagrīva 
saṃdṛṣṭo 'nāgato mayā
Bhk tvaṃ tenā'bhihitaḥ pathyaṃ kiṃ kopaṃ na niyacchasi
Bhk bhajanti vipadas tūrṇamatikrāmanti sampadaḥ
Bhk tān madān nā'vatiṣṭhante ye mate nyāyavādinām
Bhk apathyamāyatau lobhādāmanantyanujīvinaḥ
Bhk priyaṃ śṛṇoti yas tebhyas
tamṛcchanti na sampadaḥ
Bhk prājñās tejasvinaḥ samyak paśyanti ca vadanti ca
Bhk te'vajñātā mahārāja 
klāmyanti viramanti ca
Bhk leḍhi bheṣajavan nityaṃ yaḥ pathyāni kaṭūnyapi
Bhk tadarthaṃ sevate cā ''ptān
kadācin na sa sīdati
Bhk sarvasya jāyate mānaḥ
svahitāc ca pramādyati
Bhk vṛddhau bhajati cā 'pathyaṃ naro yena vinaśyati
Bhk dveṣṭi prāyo guṇebhyo yan
na ca snihyati kasyacit
Bhk vairāyate mahadbhiś ca śīyate vṛddhimānapi
Bhk samāśvasimi kenā 'haṃ
kathaṃ prāṇimi durgataḥ
Bhk lokatrayapatir bhrātā yasya me svapiti kṣitau
Bhk aho jāgarti kṛcchreṣu daivaṃ
yad balabhijjitaḥ
Bhk luṭhyanti bhūmau klidyanti bāndhavā me svapanti ca
Bhk śivāḥ kuṣṇanti māṃsāni
bhūmiḥ pibati śoṇitam
Bhk daśagrīvasanābhīnāṃ samadantyāmiṣaṃ khagāḥ
Bhk yena pūtakrator mūrdhni sthīyate sma mahā''have
Bhk tasyā'pīndrajito daivād dhvāṃkṣaiḥ śirasi līyate
Bhk svarbhānur bhāskaraṃ grastaṃ niṣṭīvati kṛtā'hnikaḥ
Bhk abhyupaiti punar bhūtiṃ rāmagrasto na kaścana
Bhk tvamajānannidaṃ rājannīḍiṣe sma svavikramam
Bhk dātuṃ necchasi sītāṃ sma
viṣayāṇāṃ ca neśiṣe
Bhk mantre jātu vadantyajñās
tvaṃ tānapyanumanyase
Bhk kathaṃ nāma bhavāṃs tatra nā 'vaiti hitamātmanaḥ
Bhk apṛṣṭo nu bravīti tvāṃ mantre mātāmaho hitam
Bhk na karomītipaulastya 
tadā mohāt tvamuktavān
Bhk tvaṃ sma vettha mahārāja 
yat smā''ha na vibhīṣanaḥ
Bhk purā tyajati yat kruddo māṃ nirākṛtya saṃsadi
Bhk havir jakṣiti niḥśaṅko makheṣu madhavānasau
Bhk pravāti svecchayā vāyurudgacchati ca bhāskaraḥ
Bhk dhanānāmīśate yakṣā
yamo dāmyati rākṣasān
Bhk tanoti varuṇaḥ pāśamindunodīyate 'dhunā
Bhk śāmyatyṛtusamāhāras
tapasyanti vanaukasaḥ
Bhk no namasyanti te bandhūn
varivasyanti nā 'marāḥ
Bhk śrīr niṣkuṣyati laṅkāyāṃ
virajyanti samṛddhayaḥ
Bhk na veda tan
na yasyā'sti mṛte tvayi viparyayaḥ
Bhk śaktiṃ saṃsvajate śakro
gopāyati hariḥ śriyam
Bhk devavandyaḥ pramodante
citrīyante
ghanodayāḥ
Bhk bibhratyastrāṇi sā'marṣā raṇakāmyanti cā 'marāḥ
Bhk cakāsati ca
māṃsā'dāṃ tathārandhreṣu jāgrati
Bhk cañcūryate 'bhito laṅkāmasmāṃś cā 'pyatiśerate
Bhk bhūmayanti svasāmarthyaṃ
kīrtiṃ naḥ kanayanti ca
Bhk diśo vyaṣnuvate dṛptās tvatkṛtāṃ jahati sthitim

hasanti tvāṃ vipadgatam

sarvāṃś cā''gāmukān drutam
Bhk gantāraḥ paramāṃ prītiṃ paurāḥ ṣrutvā vacas tava
Bhk jñātvaitat sammukhīnaś ca sametā bharato dhruvam
Bhk gate tvayi pathā 'nena vayamapyaṃhitāsmahe
Bhk labdhāhe 'haṃ dhṛtiṃ prāpte bhūyo bhavati sammukhe
Bhk gate tasmin gṛhītā 'rthe rāmaḥ sugrīvarākṣasau
Bhk uktavān śvo 'bhigantāstho yuvāṃ saha mayā puram
Bhk draṣṭāsthas tatra tisro me māt s tuṣṭa'ntarā''tmanaḥ
Bhk āntyantīnaṃ sakhitvaṃ ca prāptāstho bharatā ''śrayam
Bhk naivaṃ virahaduḥkhena vayaṃ vyāghānitāsmahe
Bhk śramo nubhavitā naivaṃ bhavadbhyāṃ ca viyogajaḥ
Bhk evaṃ yuvāṃ mama prītyai kalptāsthaḥ kapirākṣasau 
Bhk gantuṃ prayatitāsāthe prātaḥ saha mayā yadi
Bhk utkavantau tato rāmaṃ vacaḥ paulastyavānarau
Bhk anugraho 'yaṃ kākutstha 
gantāsvo yat tvayā saha
Bhk anumantāsvahe nā''vāṃ bhavantaṃ virahaṃ tvayā
Bhk api prāpya surendratvaṃ
kiṃ nu prattaṃ
tvayā ''spadam
Bhk tataḥ kathābhiḥ samatītya doṣā māruhya sainyaiḥ saha puṣpakaṃ te
Bhk samprasthitā vegavaśādagādhaṃ prakṣobhayantaḥ salilaṃ payodheḥ
Bhk setuṃ mahendraṃ
malayaṃ savindhyaṃ
samālyavantaṃ girimṛṣyamūkam
Bhk sadaṇḍakā'raṇyavātīṃ ca pampāṃ rāmaḥ priyāyāḥ kathayan jagāma
Bhk ete te munijanamaṇḍitā digantāḥ
śailo'yaṃ lulitavanaḥ sa citrakūṭaḥ
Bhk gaṅgeyaṃ sutanu
viśālatīraramyā
maithilyā raghutanayo diśan nananda
Bhk śiñjānabhramarakulā''kulā'grapuṣpāḥ śītā'mbhaḥpravilayasaṃplavā 'bhilīnāḥ
Bhk ete te sutanu 
purījanopabhogyā dṛśyante nayanamanoramā vanā 'ntāḥ
Bhk sthānaṃ naḥ pūrvajānāmiyamadhikamasau preyasī pūrayodhyā
dūrādālokyate yā hutavividhahaviḥ prīṇitā 'śeṣadevā
Bhk so 'yaṃ deśo
rudantaṃ purajanamakhilaṃ yatra hitvā prayātau āvāṃ sīte 
vanā 'ntaṃ saha dhṛtadhṛtinā lakṣmaṇena kṣapā'nte
Bhk tūryāṇāmatha niḥsvanena sakalaṃ lokaṃ samāpūrayan vikrāntaiḥ kariṇāṃ girīndrasadṛśāṃ kṣmāṃ kampayan sarvataḥ
Bhk sā ''nandā 'śruvilocanaḥ prakṛtibhiḥ sārdhaṃ sahā 'ntaḥ puraḥ samprāpto bharataḥ samārutiralaṃ namraḥ samaṃ mātṛbhiḥ
Bhk atha sasambhramapaurajanā ''vṛto bharatapāṇidhṛtojjvalacāmaraḥ
Bhk gurujanadvijabandyabhinanditaḥ praviśati sma puraṃ raghunandanaḥ
Bhk pravidhāya dhṛtiṃ parāṃ janānāṃ yuvarājaṃ bharataṃ tato'bhiṣicya
Bhk jaghaṭe turagā'dhvareṇa yaṣṭuṃ kṛtasambhāravidhiḥ patiḥ prajānām
Bhk idamadhigatamuktimārgacitraṃ vivadiṣatāṃ vadatāṃ ca sannibandhāt
Bhk janayati vijayaṃ sadā janānāṃ yudhi susamāhitamaiśvaraṃ yathā 'stram
Bhk dīpatulyaḥ prabandho 'yaṃ śabdalakṣaṇacakṣuṣām
Bhk hastā 'marṣa ivā 'ndhānāṃ bhaved vyākaraṇādṛte
Bhk vyākhyāgamyamidaṃ kāvya mutsavaḥ sudhiyāmalam
Bhk hatā durmeghasaś cā 'smin vidvatpriyatayā mayā
Bhk kāvyamidaṃ vihitaṃ mayā valabhyāṃ śrīdharasenanerandrapālitāyām
Bhk kīrtirato bhavatān nṛpasya
tasya premakaraḥ kṣitipo yataḥ prajānām
